China Signs the International Monetary Fund: Exchange Rate Fluctuations Are Restricted; Economic Experts Discuss Currency Devaluation

[Reuters, Nanjing, 23rd] Although the official solemnly declared that the exchange rate will never change, the foreign exchange market in Nanjing still fluctuates according to the Shanghai market. The street trading rate today is 3,550 yuan of legal tender for one U.S. dollar, and large bills can only be exchanged for 3,400 yuan. It seems that most people dealing in U.S. dollars are optimistic about the increase. According to an economic expert who is closely related to China's monetary system, China is a signatory country of the International Monetary Fund. The Fund stipulated a month ago that each member country should register its permanent and stable exchange rate against major gold standard currencies (i.e., the U.S. dollar, the British pound, and the French franc) with the Fund within three months after issuing the final notice. The purpose is to prevent major devaluations of national currencies before the specified deadline. After the deadline, China and every other signatory country must be bound by the registered exchange rate. If the domestic situation requires the currency to be devalued again, the devaluation value may not exceed one-tenth, and this adjustment must be implemented at least six months after registration. Responsible observers are well aware that a 13% readjustment is not enough to cope with possible and frequent devaluations. Therefore, it is necessary to announce a final devaluation once again within two months. If, unfortunately, the situation continues to deteriorate after this devaluation, China still has the right to withdraw the devaluation restriction from the International Monetary Fund. However, this move is tantamount to declaring national bankruptcy to the world, which no country would want to do.

[Associated Press, Tianjin, 23rd] After Shanghai rumors that the official exchange rate of legal tender against the U.S. dollar will be readjusted again, the market price of the U.S. dollar in the open market here has reached a new peak. As of now, the highest price is 3,610 yuan.

A Historic Feat: 150,000 Soldiers Disarm, Military Men are True Heroes, Chairman Praises the Sixth Officer Training Corps

The soldiers of the Republic of China are all aware of the importance of today's nation-building task. Our nation-building work can be fully completed (loud applause from 100,000 people in the entire venue). This is indeed a rare miracle in the 5,000-year history of the Chinese nation.

Because Emperor Gaozu of Han and Emperor Taizong of Tang did not have resettlement methods for the discharged soldiers, and Europe and the United States had reemployment methods but no vocational training, to enhance the martial virtue of the Chinese nation and solve the most dangerous and headache-inducing troop reduction problem in the 5,000-year history of the Chinese nation."

Editorial

Four Foreign Ministers Gather in Paris

The Paris Peace Conference has been going on for a month, but no agreement has been reached. All parties are concerned and eager. The war has just ended, and the opinions of various countries on rebuilding the peaceful order in Europe are not entirely the same, and they do not want to act hastily. This is exactly the phenomenon that should be present in making peace. Therefore, we should not have any feelings of disappointment about the slow progress of the Paris Peace Conference. While the Paris Peace Conference was in progress, we saw the US Secretary of State, the Soviet Foreign Minister, and the British Foreign Minister leave Paris one after another, either going to Moscow, inspecting the war zones in Germany, or returning to London. Later, we saw US Secretary of State Byrnes's speech in Germany and Soviet Foreign Minister Molotov's speech at the Peace Conference Subcommittee, each clarifying the foreign policies of the United States and the Soviet Union. At this time, US Secretary of Commerce Wallace gave a speech in the United States, advocating appeasement of the Soviet Union. As a result, public opinion was in an uproar and condemned him. Wallace had to resign. Now that Wallace has resigned, the storm caused by Wallace's speech has gradually calmed down, and the four foreign ministers have gathered in Paris again. The Paris Peace Conference, which had been suspended, may become active again, and the foreign ministers' meeting, which has been shelved for a long time, may be reconvened. Thus, after a period of suspension and turmoil, Paris will once again become the center of international diplomatic activities. Based on the developments of the past few weeks, we would like to make a forecast of international politics.

The world situation in the year since the armistice has obviously stopped all the coordination during the war due to the cessation of hostilities. Originally, the maintenance of this coordination lacked a considerable practical basis and was only a wartime compromise. In order to maintain this wartime compromise, even Roosevelt, who advocated international justice, did not hesitate to abandon his principles and his position, and not only built a high iron curtain with the Soviet Union, but also spread its "new democracy" of socialist countries outside the iron curtain. The post-war world was obviously shrouded in this atmosphere. Under this situation, Wallace advocated returning to a new "glorious isolation" and treating China as an "uncivilized land," watching the sparks of Europe and the Far East across the Pacific and Atlantic Oceans. Although the appearance of this Wallaceism is in the form of "new isolationism," it actually inherits some of the mantles of the Anglo-American appeasement policy before the Second World War. Therefore, we must seek the foreign policies of Britain and the United States from other aspects.

US Secretary of State Byrnes's speech in Stuttgart clarified the US government's enlightened policy towards post-war Europe. Later, British wartime Prime Minister Churchill also gave a speech in Switzerland, advocating the establishment of a European Federation, so that Europe could almost restore its prosperity. Churchill, as a person in opposition, cannot represent the intentions of the British government. However, the Labour Party, which is currently in power in Britain, although advocating the implementation of socialism, which is considered "unscientific" by Marxists and Leninists, cannot be compared with the Soviet Union's "new democracy." Therefore, Churchill's speech may also represent the opinions of some British people. The ideal of a European Federation is not new to Europeans. After the First World War, French politicians advocated the establishment of a European Federation, but the situation at the time turned the ideal into a dream. Now that Europe is under threat again, perhaps Europeans will feel the need for such an organization, but whether it can be formed is still in a vague state.

Will the result of this evolution make the world one world, or will it become two? In reality, one world is only a lofty ideal, and the real gap has long existed! The world is a troubled time. We certainly do not want to see the distance of the gap widening, but rather pray that everyone should fill this gap at this time. However, in the effort to fill this gap, we have the right to demand that all major countries should make concessions for the safety of all mankind, and we must not rely solely on our side, or even sacrifice the principles we uphold like President Roosevelt in order to accommodate reality. How to make efforts to fill this gap depends on the achievements of the foreign ministers in Paris.

The Door to US-Soviet Cooperation

Wallace's resignation was discussed in this newspaper yesterday. We are planning for the overall situation of the world, and we certainly feel that Wallace's speech cannot represent the US government's foreign policy, so the US government has the need to ask him to step down in order to seek consistency between foreign policy and external policy. However, in any case, we are still very sorry for the occurrence of this unfortunate fact. Because the door to US-Soviet cooperation seems to be separated by a layer of curtains again.

Here, we would like to state another view: Wallace's foreign policy is to make concessions to the Soviet Union, and Byrnes's foreign policy is to be tough on the Soviet Union. This difference is very obvious. Can concessions win the cooperation of the Soviet Union? Can toughness win the submission of the Soviet Union? No one can predict these two points. However, Byrnes's tough policy, to this day, seems not only to have failed to make the Soviet Union dare to symbolize it, but has instead made the barriers between the United States and the Soviet Union increasingly sharp. Wallace's foreign policy, standing in the position of the Americans, seems to have the necessity of trying.

The two biggest points in Wallace's speech and letter to Truman are that he did not have a definite grasp of the serious problem that the United States and the Soviet Union do not trust each other because of the differences in political and economic systems, except that he himself "firmly believed" that it could be solved. The opposition between the United States and the Soviet Union, as pointed out in this newspaper's editorial on the 19th, is a conflict between two kinds of democracy. In other words, it is a conflict between American democracy and Soviet communism. Wallace's plan for US-Soviet reconciliation purely focuses on military and economic aspects, and ignores the lofty ideals of human politics. Wallace was originally an agricultural expert and served as Secretary of Commerce, specializing in agriculture and commerce. People who pay attention to the superficial phenomena of human life tend to ignore the ideological activities of human beings that promote the realization of superficial phenomena.

Thought is the source of phenomena. According to Hegel's view, the human spirit, with the evolution of history, demands its own realization everywhere and at all times. Now the struggle between the United States and the Soviet Union, the struggle between the two major groups in the world, is not a struggle between atomic bombs and naval bases and ports, but a struggle between two great ideologies demanding their own realization. The fourteen communist leaders in the Kremlin, in order to realize their ideas inherited from Marx, will not hesitate to pay any price, take any means, and no international treaty can bind them. Under this situation, unless American society undergoes a fundamental revolution and becomes a Soviet-style "new democracy," US-Soviet cooperation is still uncertain. Even Wallace himself did not tell the American people how much certainty there was.

However, Soviet-style "new democracy" is not welcomed by Americans except for a very small number of communists. Not only capitalists do not welcome it, but even workers do not necessarily welcome it. The United States today is the most prosperous country, and the living standards of its people are higher than anywhere else in the world. Since life is comfortable and they enjoy a high degree of democratic freedom, among all the workers in the world, American workers have the least awareness of communist revolution. And the United States has no hope at all. Even in other democratic countries, unless it is within its own military range, there is no hope. The Greek referendum is a clear example. Human beings certainly want to live, but they also want freedom. The biggest flaw of Soviet-style "new democracy" is that the people have no freedom!

Some people believe that Wallace's speech was a probe from the White House in the United States. The US government is unwilling to go to war and is willing to cooperate with the Soviet Union, but any cooperation is not a one-sided matter. Since the US President let Wallace give a speech, if the Soviet Union has a sincere response to cooperation, the US's tough foreign policy towards the Soviet Union may gradually change. If this observation is correct, then President Truman's request for Wallace to resign is exactly his expression of disappointment after hope! Because since Wallace's speech was published, in addition to praising Wallace and scolding Byrnes, the Soviet official newspaper has not made any concrete statements on the part of the government. Under such an attitude of the Soviet Union, President Truman has no reason to adopt Wallace's suggestion and offer the secret of the atomic bomb to Marshal Stalin with both hands.

We are very sorry for Wallace's resignation, because his speech did open the door to US-Soviet cooperation once, but now that the guest is not coming and Wallace has resigned, this door seems to be closed again. However, we still hope that this door can be opened again at any time, and we believe that it will be opened again one day. In China, we pray even more that the door to US-Soviet cooperation will open sooner. The people in power in the United States may as well learn more about the Soviet Union and study the background of communist thought. The Soviet leaders may as well walk out of the Kremlin and take a look at the true face of the world. When they understand each other, it will be the time when world peace truly sprouts.

The Necessity of Suppressing High Interest Rates

High interest rates are one of the most troublesome problems currently faced by the industrial and commercial sectors.

On one hand, there is inflation, and on the other hand, there is a sense of excess capital with no way out. According to normal theory, interest rates on short-term loans should be low at this time, and high interest rates should not occur. However, theory is theory, and reality is reality. This kind of contradictory phenomenon is not the only one in the current economic sphere.

As a result, the Four Banks' tight monetary policy has attracted special attention from the general public. All kinds of loans are being applied for continuously by various industries and businesses in various places; the deposit and withdrawal amounts of commercial firms and banks are also being discussed; whether loans of more than 50 million must be approved by the Four Banks is also being criticized; and some people have even raised the fundamental question of whether the Four Banks themselves should continue to exist.

There are, of course, legitimate reasons for the Four Banks to tighten the money supply and refuse to lend. Judging from the intention, stabilizing prices and avoiding further stimulation are the main reasons. Recalling the beginning of the establishment of the grain loan, within two or three days, rice prices in various places experienced a great surge. Therefore, their cautious attitude can also be said to be well-founded.

However, the existence of high interest rates is a fact, the difficulty of turnover felt by the general industrial and commercial sectors is also a fact, and the closure of many factories and shops is even more of a fact. It is said that the current interest rate in Japan is only about two percent, and in Taiwan it is only about six percent. Then, whether the short-term interest rate of one and a half or even two percent in this port is too high for the industrial and commercial sectors that need to compete with others, and whether it should be improved, really does not need further discussion. Have those officials and financial giants who preside over the Four Banks never thought of this?

There are two main reasons for high prices: one is inflation, and the other is insufficient supply. These are the most obvious facts. Because of the result of tightening the money supply, many production industries have been unable to sustain themselves; the supply of materials will inevitably gradually decrease in the future. Is this situation indirectly raising prices? This issue should not be ignored!

Moreover, the rising trend of prices does not seem to be stopped or reversed by tightening the money supply. In recent days, major commodities such as gold, U.S. dollars, yarn, cloth, rice, wheat, flour, cooking oil, woolen cloth, and rayon have not been soaring again? On the one hand, the rising trend remains the same, and tightening the money supply does not have the slightest inhibitory effect. On the other hand, it has forced industrial and commercial sectors to collapse and indirectly promoted the rising trend. We believe that this approach has indeed reached the stage where it should "correct mistakes when they are known". Be careful not to stubbornly continue to make mistakes to the end, causing China's industrial and commercial sectors to be destroyed.

Central Bank's "Hundred Cities Edition" Banknotes Still Accepted and Used as Usual

[Central News Agency, Nanjing, 23rd] Recently, merchants and residents in this city have often mentioned that the Central Bank's 1,000-yuan and 500-yuan banknotes printed by the Fuda Printing Bureau in Southeast provinces and Fujian in the 34th year of the Republic of China are not woodblock prints. Five Major Traitors, Including Zhou Fohai and Ding Mocun, Were Officially Escorted and Imprisoned Yesterday. Zhou Wore Black Gauze on His Arm, Seeming to Mourn for Wang Jingwei.

[Our Newspaper, Nanjing, 23rd] The "escort" procedures for the five major traitors, including Zhou Fohai, were completed on the 23rd. At 12:30 noon, Chen Shengzu, a prosecutor from the Capital High Court, and eight bailiffs took a large open car to the detention center at No. 19 Ninghai Road to complete the transfer procedures. First, Chen and Director Zhang discussed everything in detail. At 2:30 p.m., the bailiffs were ordered to set up posts at the door and roadside. Then, they moved the luggage onto the car. At 3:00 p.m., the traitors came out one after another. Zhou led the way holding a palm-leaf fan, followed by Luo and others. Each person was monitored by a bailiff. The clothes and attitudes of the traitors were as follows: Zhou wore a Palissy long gown, with black gauze wrapped around his left arm, seeming to mourn for Wang Jingwei, black leather-soled shoes, and a felt hat. Luo wore a gray striped short suit, yellow leather shoes with elastic sides, and a gray felt hat, with a cunning smile on his face. Ding wore a black felt hat, a blue cloth long gown, black cloth-soled shoes, and carried a small white package in his hand. His face was pale, his expression was dejected, and his eyes were dull. Ma wore a dark blue striped fine wool long gown and had a stiff attitude. The traitors carried a total of nine large packages, three suitcases, a large can of biscuits, and two thermos bottles, for a total of thirteen items. Yesterday, Ma's wife brought ten packages, and it was said that there were still three suitcases and many other scattered items. The prison authorities were worried about criticism from others, so they temporarily left them behind. A quarter of an hour after Zhou left, Ma's wife, female nurse, and maid came to visit. They were very distressed to hear that he had been escorted away. They immediately wanted to take the luggage away, but the prison authorities agreed that they could come to pick it up tomorrow morning. After leaving Ninghai Road, they went straight to the detention center of the Capital District Court at Laohuqiao. Then, because the detention center was also overcrowded, they began interrogation and inspected the luggage at the same time, which was completed at night. It is said that the five traitors were separately detained in Cell Nos. 4 and 6 of the Loyalty Prison. According to Director Wan, they will enjoy the same treatment as ordinary prisoners and will not be allowed to take any special actions.

"Coolie" Chinese Laborers Return Home from Bangka Island

The Dutch Break Their Promise and Shamefully Abandon Them

[Central News Agency, Singapore, 23rd] Before the war, from 1935 to 1941, there were more than 4,000 so-called "coolie" Chinese laborers on Bangka Island near Sumatra. They accepted contracts with the Dutch government to work in the tin mines on Bangka Island. During the Japanese occupation, they were severely abused, resulting in the death of more than half of them. Currently, because the contracts have expired, their situation is very difficult and pitiful. They all wish to return home. The Dutch have decided to send them back in batches. The first batch of 1,300 people left Bangka Island on the 21st of this month. One of the workers told reporters that according to the contract terms, the Dutch should provide full travel expenses for those who have served for two years, as well as a subsidy, a pair of shoes, and a hat, but the Dutch broke their promise and only promised to issue ten guilders per person when they arrived in Hong Kong. Whether the Dutch will keep their promise is doubtful. Overseas Chinese in the banking sector have raised donations and distributed three and a half guilders to each person.

These remarks made by Mr. Zhou, a communist official, are obviously purely for propaganda purposes, and their purpose is obviously to undermine the reputation of the United States as much as possible. If Mr. Zhou is really concerned about the erroneous image of the Chinese economic situation, then he can easily list its real causes, because he, like other people, has clearly observed that the causes are not mysterious at all. The first and most important cause is that the Chinese government has lost all its best sources of revenue while in office, so it has to rely on issuing banknotes to survive, which has caused terrible inflation. The second reason is that the conflict between the Nationalists and Communists has delayed economic recovery, part of which is due to the effective cutting of transportation lines by the Communist army. The third reason is the inefficiency or corruption (or both) of many officials in the government. The fourth is the Soviet Union's destruction or removal of industrial equipment in the Northeast. Mr. Zhou instead attributes this to the United States, arguing that after some U.S. surplus materials were handed over to the Chinese government, they flowed into the black market. If this statement is true, it is not important except in Shanghai and most other cities. If it is said that China's suffering is due to the United States selling materials that its army and navy no longer use to China, then this statement can fully demonstrate its unreasonableness and senselessness.

[Our Newspaper, Hangzhou, 23rd] The Zhejiang Provincial Council held its 17th meeting today and passed the provincial budget plan. After the reform of the Zhejiang provincial fiscal revenue and expenditure system, revenue has decreased due to the abolition of harsh and miscellaneous taxes, and the resumption of conscription has made it impossible to balance. The Four-Power Foreign Ministers Conference Reopens; Bevin Meets with Molotov Yesterday; The Conference Discusses the Issue of Former Italian Territories

[Our Newspaper] London, 23rd (broadcast): British Foreign Secretary Bevin met with Soviet Foreign Minister Molotov this afternoon and then met with Bidault to discuss convening a Four-Power Foreign Ministers Conference. According to the BBC, the Four-Power Foreign Ministers Conference will be convened within 24 hours.

Another dispatch: The Four-Power Foreign Ministers issued a declaration today agreeing to submit the issue of Italy's African colonies to the UN General Assembly for a decision.

[Our Newspaper] Paris, 23rd (broadcast): The main part of the peace treaty with Italy began to be discussed at the conference this morning, namely Article 17 of the peace treaty, the issue of former Italian colonies. The original four-power draft contained three points: (1) Italy should renounce its rights to its former colonies; (2) the existing government authorities, namely the "British and French Military Government," should continue until the fate of these colonies is definitively resolved; (3) the four powers will decide the fate of former Italian colonies within a one-year period after the signing of the peace treaty with Italy. Representatives of various countries then expressed their opinions one after another. Italian representative Bonomi said that Italians have a historical action in Africa, and now more than 100,000 Italians reside in the various territories, forming the basis of the economic foundation of the various territories. Italians cannot give up these colonies without any legal protection. Bonomi then expressed his gratitude for the Soviet and French suggestions to the Four-Power Foreign Ministers Conference to change the political system of the former Italian colonies into a trusteeship! He also requested that the Italian delegation be allowed to continue to participate in the work of the government in its African colonies. Representatives from Egypt and Abyssinia requested the return of the Istrian territory. Egypt also requested the Kalfu grass source in Libya and the Solun Plateau in Libya at the same time. The Egyptian representative further proposed that Libya be governed by the member states of the Arab League. Abyssinia stated that it was willing to temporarily give up the former Italian colony of Somalia, but reserved the right to express its views on this issue in the future. The Brazilian representative supported the proposal to place the former Italian colonies under trusteeship, but this would become an amendment to Article 17 of the peace treaty. New Zealand requested that the fate of the Italian territories not be decided solely by the four powers, but should be decided by the United Nations.

Large and small countries attack each other, and the words used are unprecedented in diplomacy, but I believe that the disputes will eventually be overcome. The world has high hopes for the UN Charter, but unfortunately it has failed to live up to the expectations of the world. Even the wartime industries of ten countries are still producing as usual, resulting in a very dangerous rumor that the so-called Third World War is inevitable. Fortunately, we still maintain an optimistic attitude and are not attacked by fear and deterioration. Regarding Switzerland's neutral position, the UN Charter will inevitably impose the obligations borne by UN member states on our country, but our country is in a neutral position, and it is difficult to fulfill them. Therefore, no one knows when Switzerland will be able to join the UN organization. However, there is also a possibility that it can be realized in the shortest possible time, and the site of the women's UN organization may use the old League of Nations site in Geneva.

US Assists Japan in Restoring Industrial Economy; Japanese Cocoon Shipment to China Rejected; Textile Advisor of MacArthur Issues Statement

[Associated Press, Tokyo, 23rd] MacArthur's headquarters textile advisor, Magana, today accused Song Ziwen, the President of the Executive Yuan of China, and stated that he opposed the shipment of any silkworm cocoons to China. It is understood that the Chinese delegation to Japan had requested the shipment of 1.5 million pounds of Japanese silkworm cocoons to China, which was rejected by MacArthur's headquarters. They recently expressed dissatisfaction and indirectly accused American capitalists of attempting to seize Japan's silk industry, which aroused Magana's reaction. According to Magana, the main source of funds for the occupation forces paid by Japan comes from Japan's silk weaving industry, so the plan was not fulfilled. Chinese silk factories purchased a large batch of low-quality silkworm cocoons domestically earlier this year, believing that the silk made from these silkworm cocoons could be sold at high prices in the United States or international markets. The Chinese side attempted to obtain better-quality Japanese silkworm cocoons at a low price to offset the funds spent on purchasing silkworm cocoons in their own country earlier. Japan is in need of all its silkworm cocoons to maintain raw silk exports. Some Japanese silk factories are currently being urged to switch to producing cotton and rayon fabrics, which is also for this reason. Orders have now been given to the Japanese to expand mulberry fields to increase the amount of silkworm cocoons so that annual raw silk exports can reach 30 million pounds. Before the war, Japan exported 95 million pounds of raw silk annually. China currently has silkworm mercury that can produce 20,000 packages of raw silk annually, but China has not yet achieved this. The Chinese delegation's request to ship Japanese silkworm mercury to China came from a direct request from the Chinese silk company to the delegation. American merchants have never used the government to request MacArthur's headquarters to obtain Japanese export commodities for them. Any silkworm cocoons shipped to China will further harm Japan's economy. Therefore, shipping Japanese silkworm cocoons to China would violate the Potsdam Declaration and would not be in line with the purpose of occupying Japan.

[Associated Press, Washington, 22nd] The US government's assistance to Japan in restoring its industrial economy is proceeding steadily. This matter involves the cooperation of the State Department, the Army Department, and other government agencies to ensure that Japan quickly restores its economic position, at least to the point of self-sufficiency, and to pay for the United Nations occupation expenses with the help of experts. Japan's textile industry, cotton yarn industry, and rayon industry have all received strong assistance. The US government is purchasing all the raw silk that Japan can produce and will provide more assistance to its rayon industry to revive it. For several months, raw cotton has been continuously imported into Japan, and funds have been provided to purchase foreign goods that Japan urgently needs. However, Japan's re-entry into the cotton fabric export market has not been unanimously approved by the United Nations. In the Far East, India needs cotton fabrics, and Japanese yarn factories are willing to supply them. However, China, Britain, and other producers hope to restore their pre-war business. According to the views of the US authorities, despite opposition from all parties, large-scale assistance will continue to be provided to the Japanese textile industry.

Estimated Production Capacity of Japanese Cotton Cloth

[French News Agency, Washington, 21st] The US military government in the Japanese-occupied area recently announced in a report that an agreement has been established between the Japanese textile industry, Japanese banks, and the Ministry of Finance to establish a banking group to fund the activities of the cotton weaving industry. Before the war, Japan sold more than 3 million yards of cotton cloth in the world market annually. It is expected that Japan will resume exports by the end of this year, most of which will be cotton fabrics, raw silk, and cotton yarn spun from American cotton. The US government agency, Commodity Credit Corporation, will supply Japan with 890,000 bales of cotton this year, of which 185,384 bales have already been shipped. This cotton will all be woven into cotton fabric for export. Eighty percent of Japanese spindles were destroyed due to the war, which greatly reduced cotton cloth production, but it is expected that production capacity can be doubled by the end of 1947. The production of cotton yarn is limited due to the lack of coal and chemicals, but the production of yarn pulp has greatly increased. The production of raw silk this year is approximately 150 million yards, but only 30 million yards are prepared for export. Japanese silk industry exporters expect that within five years, Japan's raw silk exports can restore its leading position in the world market. It is reported that the United States, Britain, and the Soviet Union are willing to encourage the revival of Japan's textile export industry for different reasons. The United States hopes that Japan will use textile exports to pay for imported food and occupation expenses; Britain needs Japan to supply cotton fabrics to British territories; and the Soviet Union hopes to obtain Japanese textiles under a barter system. Therefore, the Japanese textile industry has a prosperous outlook.

Modern "Tarzan" Grows Up Among Antelopes; Walks as Fast as the Wind; Does Not Understand Human Language; Makes Goat Sounds and Eats Grass

[Reuters, Bata, 22nd] The antelope man recently discovered in the outer Jordanian desert is now being carefully cared for by Gilbert of the Iraqi Oil Company. According to Gilbert, when this 15-year-old strange man was captured, he ran at a speed of 50 miles per hour, which is more than twice the world short-distance record of 100 yards. This modern "Tarzan" is thought to have been abandoned by his mother when he was young and adopted by a group of antelopes, gradually learning various characteristics of antelopes. I have studied him in detail and found that his actions, cries, and so on are all like domestic antelopes. He is only willing to eat grass and does not want to eat ordinary food. But I am sure that he is a human being, but he grew up among domestic antelopes. He almost lost his life when he was first discovered by hunters of antelopes. Fortunately, one person in the shadows saw a child in the flock of sheep and immediately greeted his companions not to shoot, and then drove a car to chase him, and the child ran at a speed of 50 miles per hour, and finally fell to the ground. According to the chief of the Ruhwala tribe, who first took care of the child, the child jumped on the roof on the first day in his home, and then jumped from one roof to another, and then jumped into the street. Finally, he dispatched vehicles and horses to chase him, and he was captured after more than two hours. When the child was first discovered, there were many rumors, some saying that he was half human and half goat. Now we know that the child is indeed human, but he is more robust than ordinary people. Of course, he cannot speak human language, he can only make antelope cries. It is said that he has recently become accustomed to human life. It is said that mothers of nomadic peoples in the Near East often abandon their children to herds of beasts, but most of them are eaten by beasts, and it is rare for them to be raised by beasts.

The Mystery of the Middle East (Part 1)

— Originally written by Pasil, translated by Wen Hao

On the international stage, the Middle East is about to show its skills again. Here, Britain and Russia are opposed to each other, the United States stands on the side of Britain, and Diego is also eager to step onto the stage. She has recently acted as a mediator several times. As for the people of the Middle East, not long ago, they were bought off and had no idea what was going on in the play. But now the situation is different. The representatives of the people, whether real or fake, often hold a considerable position on this stage. The key to the Middle East is in the hands of Britain and Russia. Britain is deeply afraid that Russia's encouragement of leftist elements in the Near East will threaten the lifeline of the British Empire. Conversely, Russia is deeply afraid that Britain will use reactionary forces to create a government to make things difficult for it.

Difficulties are brewing everywhere in the Middle East. The factors can be divided into three categories: Conflicts of interest between Britain, the United States, France, and the Soviet Union; In the past 30 years, a high degree of nationalism has deeply grasped Islam; Due to frequent contact with the West during World War II, a kind of social awakening was created, and this awakening was further accelerated by the socialism brought by Russia.

Since the birth of civilization, geography and history have bestowed the Middle East with supreme strategic importance because it is a bridge and a transverse road between many continents. It is a part of Asia and a necessary path for Westerners to come to the East. It contains the richest oil mines in the world and many other undeveloped resources. The three powers are very clear: Any country that controls the Middle East alone will eventually be able to control Asia and its 1.2 billion people, which is almost half of the world's population.

Turkey and the Straits

Gongguo is deeply afraid that Russia's influence will enter the Mediterranean Sea through the Tartar Neil Strait and the Persian Gulf through Iran. Britain believes that this intrusion is very unfavorable. In order to resist this intrusion, Britain often asks Russia to respect the territorial integrity of Turkey and Iran in the same way. With the support of the United States, Britain has gained greater trust from the conservative governments of Turkey and Iran. Conversely, Russia is also promoting that Britain and the United States are trying to control the politics and economy of the entire Middle East. Russia believes that it is not only excluded from the Middle East oil mines but also needs sea and air bases to resist the military encirclement formed by Britain there, which have been rejected everywhere. With the collapse of the French and Italian navies today, the Mediterranean Sea has become a British lake. The Soviet Union has been demanding its rights to the Tartar Neil Strait. If the Tartar Neil Strait falls into the hands of Russia, Britain will be unable to prevent the pro-Russian party in Greece from seizing power. Therefore, Turkey, like Greece, has formed a key to British foreign policy.

Iranian Incident

Iran also lies on the lifeline of the British Empire. Iran's coastline forms the entire eastern part of the Persian Gulf. Iraq, Kuwait, and Saudi Arabia are located in its northern and western regions. As early as 1914, Kuwait became an independent sheikhdom under British protection, and the King of Saudi Arabia has maintained friendly relations with Britain since taking power. According to the exclusive agreement signed in March 1892, these sheikhdoms, their monarchs themselves, and their successors shall not enter into agreements or dealings with countries other than Britain, nor shall they accept ambassadors from any country other than Britain, nor shall they cede or sell any land to countries other than Britain.

Therefore, through these treaties, Britain has fully grasped the strategic advantage in the Persian Gulf. Any power that occupies a place in southern Iran can interfere with Britain's communication lines in the Arabian Sea. It can advance east and knock on the door of North India. The reason why Russian troops entered Iran after March 2 this year and Britain roared in the United Nations Security Council is here.

City Government Budget Deficit Passes 2.21 Billion Yuan, Decides on Ways to Make Up the Difference, Imposes Municipal Construction Surtax, Assembly Postponed Again, Horse Racing Issue to be Discussed Today

[Report from Our Newspaper] The Municipal Council held its 21st meeting yesterday morning. First, a memorial week was held, with Speaker Pan Gongzhan delivering a speech: The city government budget was discussed last Saturday and some resolutions have been made, but there is no final decision on the overall budget. Therefore, the budget decision should be made first on today's agenda. At the same time, it is hoped that in the morning meeting, the additional tax cases related to the budget will be discussed and decided based on the review reports, so as to make up for the budget deficit. If we only pass the budget without deciding on the remedies, the passed budget will still be nominal. Secondly, only half of the review reports of the various committees of this council have been discussed. If the agenda for postponement today (that is, yesterday) cannot be completed, the assembly may be postponed for one or two days. Finally, Mr. Pan hoped that all councilors could consistently adhere to the spirit of not being late and not asking for leave during this assembly, so as not to affect the meeting and to be responsible to the voters. According to Mr. Pan's report, the number of councilors attending the first few days of the assembly was more than 150, while later attendees were only about 110 to 120.

At the morning meeting, the Council discussed the tax cases submitted by the mayor. After discussion, it was resolved to cancel the additional defense corps uniform fees and epidemic prevention funds in the housing tax, reducing a total of 1.8 billion yuan. When incorporated into the budget revenue, the total revenue and expenditure deficit reached 22.1 billion yuan. As for the way to increase revenue, the entertainment tax was still raised to 50%, but the collection of sanitation tax was rejected. At the same time, the collection of additional tax on public utilities (excluding water tax) for half a year was approved, which can bring in 4 billion yuan. The housing tax is collected at 20% of the actual rent, to be borne by the landlord. In the afternoon, the meeting discussed who should bear the municipal surtax. The situation was quite heated, and it was decided that the municipal surtax should be borne by the residents according to the housing tax collection method.

The assembly finally passed the organizational regulations of various committees of the Municipal Council. Each committee shall have one chairman and two vice-chairmen, who shall be elected by the committee members. The chairman shall not concurrently serve as the director of the labor union. The term of office shall be three months and shall be re-elected after each assembly adjournment. Each councilor shall participate in at least one committee and at most two committees. Each committee shall meet once every two weeks, and the chairman shall convene extraordinary meetings when necessary.

In addition, as there were still many proposals to be discussed, the assembly decided to adjourn to today. Today's agenda will include discussion of social, educational, public works, regulations and "horse racing" issues, and the adoption of the assembly declaration.

Revenue and Expenditure Deficit! How to Make Up for It

Two Focal Points of Discussion

The morning session continued to discuss the city's budget for the second half of the year, focusing on: (1) How much should the revenue and expenditure deficit be determined? (2) What new tax rules should be adopted to make up for this deficit?

Before determining the deficit number, several questions were raised regarding certain existing tax systems and city government revenue items:

Travelers Should Fulfill Tax Obligations

Wu Zhengjue first asked whether the inn tax of more than 200 million yuan listed in the budget was reasonable. Gu Chunfan, Director of the Finance Bureau, immediately explained that travelers to Shanghai enjoy the city's municipal facilities and should naturally fulfill a part of their tax obligations.

The speaker explained that the interim council had already decided to collect the inn tax last time, so there was no need to discuss it again. However, Jin Runxiang and others raised it again. The speaker put it to a vote, and only a very few people agreed to cancel it.

Zhang Xuelian asked whether the city government's income from the sale of materials, 4 billion yuan, and the income from various public utilities were included in the budget. Sun Yunfeng then asked whether the materials received by the city government's Materials Receiving and Management Office were also included in the budget. Regarding these points, the mayor immediately stood up to reply that more than 90% of the 4 billion yuan from the sale of materials had been used for civil servants' living subsidies in the first half of the year. As for public property, most of the property rights involved foreign affairs issues and were awaiting designation by the Executive Yuan's management committee to resolve. As for the received materials, they would be included in the Enemy and Puppet Property Management Office in the future, so they could not be included in the budget.

Canceling Housing Tax Surcharge Increases Budget Deficit

Xu Yongzuo pointed out that the last assembly had resolved to cancel the defense corps uniform fee in the housing tax, but the entertainment tax also had this uniform fee, with a monthly income of 400 million yuan. If collection is stopped from September, the deficit will increase by 1.6 billion yuan. If the collected fees for July and August also have to be refunded, the increased deficit will be 2.4 billion yuan.

Regarding this issue, Director Gu explained again that the defense corps uniform fee attached to the housing tax was listed separately under the "temporary receipts" account, but the one attached to the entertainment tax had never been separated and was always collected and disbursed together. If it is canceled, it will cause difficulties. In fact, the dispute over the entertainment tax is not about whether the uniform fee is attached to it, but about the percentage of the tax rate. The entertainment industry has repeatedly requested a reduction in the tax rate. What the Council needs to decide now is whether to maintain the current tax rate of 40% of the ticket price or to restore it to the previous 30%. However, in any case, the deficit increased due to the reduction in the tax rate will still have to be raised from the citizens, so instead of collecting it anyway, he believes that more should be collected from those who have the money to enjoy entertainment!

The speaker read out the central government's decree on banquets and entertainment tax, which stipulates that the entertainment tax shall not exceed 50% of the ticket price. Therefore, he said: "The current budget only lists 40% of the ticket price, which does not exceed the regulations. If it is reduced, it will cause the entire city to increase the burden, which is wrong! It should be borne by those who can afford to enjoy entertainment!" Yan Kuasheng suggested that the fine item in the budget could be increased by 300 million yuan, but Feng Youzhen opposed it. He believes that there must be violations before there are fines. If the prescribed amount is too high, there may be cases of abuse of fines in the future.

Deficit of 22.1 Billion Yuan Approved by 110 Votes

The discussion of details had taken up a lot of time. The speaker finally decided to put the fundamental principle, that is, the determination of the revenue and expenditure deficit, to a vote. The original budget compiled by the city government had a deficit of 33.3 billion yuan. After the review by the ninth subcommittee, the income was increased as it should be, and the expenditures were decreased as they should be. The approved income was more than 55.1 billion yuan, the expenditures were more than 75.4 billion yuan, and the deficit was 20.3 billion yuan. However, because the last assembly resolved to cancel the defense corps uniform fee and epidemic prevention funds attached to the housing tax, which totaled 1.8 billion yuan, the income was reduced and the deficit increased to 22.1 billion yuan. If this number is passed, it will be necessary to plan ways to increase revenue to make up for it. Do the councilors agree? The result of the vote was that 110 of the 119 people present raised their hands in favor, and the principle was passed.

Three Ways to Increase Revenue: Housing Tax to be Borne by Landlords, Entertainment Tax Raised to 50%, Additional Tax on Public Utilities Levied

After the deficit of 22.1 billion yuan was determined by vote, the assembly discussed how to increase revenue to make up for it. Among the five methods submitted by the mayor, except for the horse racing tax, which would be discussed separately, the review committees believed that the municipal surtax and the public utility surtax should be adopted.

According to the report of Lu Shidao, convener of the third subcommittee, the review process was based on three principles: (1) Do not make the citizens feel that there are excessive taxes, (2) The tax standard is proportional to wealth, (3) The collection is simple and there will be no leakage. After discussion, it was felt that raising the housing tax was easier for citizens to accept, but it clearly conflicted with central government regulations and might affect the increase in rent. The sanitation tax was too trivial. The public utility surtax was the fairest and most reasonable, and the collection was the easiest, but the amount was too small. Although the municipal surtax had cumbersome collection procedures, it was relatively in line with the principle of fairness, so it was initially decided to adopt the municipal surtax method. However, after the passage, someone in the subcommittee proposed a reconsideration. As a result of the reconsideration, although the original decision was maintained, the number of votes in favor and against differed by only one vote. Later, some private individuals suggested using the name of the municipal construction surtax, which included the 4 billion yuan of the public utility surtax, and the remaining deficit of more than 18 billion yuan would be collected by the Finance Bureau according to the current housing tax ratio by adjusting the tax rate.

After Mr. Lu finished his report, the councilors expressed their opinions and the discussion was very intense. The important points are as follows:

(1) Regarding the public utility surtax, some people believe that the water tax should not be collected because water is a necessity for any common people. Some people believe that the collection of electricity tax should take into account the situation of the industry, because factories use the most electricity, especially yarn factories, and the fees are also higher, so if you want to cultivate industry, the collection of electricity tax should be considered.

The Name is Not Correct and the Words are Not Reasonable

(2) The most important thing is the opposition to the name of the municipal surtax. Tong Xingbai believes that the municipal surtax is actually a property tax, which is collected according to the value of real estate, which is in line with the Three Principles of the People's policy of controlling capital. However, the name of the municipal surtax is too vague, and he advocated changing it to property tax. He said: "I hope that the taxes in the future will be concentrated on real estate and real property, and there is no need to scrape the common people's heads in bits and pieces!" But the speaker pointed out that the collection object of the municipal surtax is the residents, not the owners. Therefore, if you want to collect property tax, that is another matter and cannot be combined with the municipal surtax. Wang Jian'e proposed that in the past, during the era of the Public Works Bureau, the housing tax was called the municipal surtax. Now that there is a housing tax, if you collect the municipal surtax again, it will give the citizens a bad impression. He advocated changing the name to the municipal construction surtax. Many people who spoke up one after another believed that the name of the property tax was not true to its name and might cause an increase in rent, so it was better to use the municipal construction surtax.

(3) Chen Gongda also proposed another way to increase revenue. He believes that since the law stipulates that the entertainment tax can be up to 50%, and the current list is only 40%, it can be increased by another 10%, so that from October to the end of December, tax revenue can be increased by 800 million to 1 billion yuan.

(4) Xu Yongzuo proposed that since the defense corps uniform fee and epidemic prevention funds have been removed from the housing tax and the collection has been reduced, the burden method should be improved. It should be collected at 30% of the actual rent according to the central government regulations, and the landlord should bear it.

Passed Three Important Resolutions

After several tens of minutes of discussion, various opinions were summarized and put to a vote. Finally, three important resolutions were passed: First, the entertainment tax rate was raised to 50%. Second, the housing tax was changed to be collected at 20% of the actual rent, and the landlord should bear it. Third, an additional tax on public utilities was levied. The remaining deficit was made up by the city government in the name of the municipal construction surtax by adjusting the tax rate.

Finally, the meeting discussed the collection method of the municipal construction surtax. Should it be borne by the landlord? Or should it be borne by the tenant? Or should the landlord and tenant bear it together?

Opinions were clearly divided into three factions: One faction believed that the landlord should bear more of the burden. Their argument was that since the landlord has real estate, he is of course a rich class, and the rich should pay more taxes! One faction believes that the municipal construction surtax is in name and in fact for municipal construction. According to the principle of equal rights and obligations, it should be borne by the people who enjoy the benefits. Now that the housing tax has been decided to be borne by the landlord, the municipal construction surtax should be borne by the tenant. The compromise faction, which is in between these two factions, advocated setting a ratio for the landlord and tenant to bear fairly.

The debate was heated, and the meeting was extended to 12:45 pm without any results. Finally, Xi Yushu suggested that the concrete figures should be discussed in the afternoon before a decision is made.

Those Who Attend the Assembly Are Not Responsible for Any External Statements, and a Statement is Made Regarding the Allocation of Temples

[Report from Our Newspaper] Since the Council passed the Minzi No. 3 Review Report resolution "Allocating or Borrowing Temples or Public Buildings" for use as district offices a few days ago, the Council has received many petitions from various temples and Buddhist associations.

Yesterday afternoon, Speaker Pan made two solemn statements at the assembly:

(1) According to Article 18 of the Council's Organizational Regulations, those who attend and attend the meeting are responsible to the Council for their speeches and are not responsible for any external statements.

(2) Regarding the Council's Minzi No. 3 Review Report resolution to allocate or borrow temples or public buildings for use as district offices, the so-called allocation was carefully considered at the time. Temples that belong to the local public or are publicly managed, and those that are currently abandoned, can be allocated. As for general temples, their consent should be obtained first and then borrowed. On the one hand, the property rights of the temples should be protected, and on the other hand, the district offices can solve all allocation or borrowing procedures. It is undoubtedly necessary to follow the provisions of the law.

[Report from Our Newspaper] Shanghai merchants Xie Xiqing, Cai Jianquan, Lu Zhonghou, Zhou Yinquan, witnesses Chen Zhixin, Yao Shaoxiu, and Xu Honghan, have jointly reported De Wu, the abbot of Jing'an Temple, and the resident monk Mi Jia for the crime of colluding with the enemy, and have filed a complaint with the High Prosecutor's Office. Discussing Municipal Construction Surtax, Resolved to be Borne by Residents

Yesterday afternoon, the Municipal Council continued to discuss the issue of who should bear the municipal construction surtax. The councilors engaged in an unprecedentedly heated debate over whether it should be borne by the tenants or jointly by the landlords and tenants, and most of them used actual figures as a basis.

The final resolution passed was: "(1) The municipal construction surtax shall be collected in accordance with the method of the Father No. 2 proposal. Of the total amount, in addition to the housing tax collected at 20% of the actual rent, which shall be borne by the landlord, the remainder shall be stipulated as the donation rate for setting up the donation. It is divided into three grades according to the current value of the house: Grade A, with a current value of 100 million yuan or more, shall be charged a monthly donation of 3/1000. Grade B, with a current value of 50 million yuan or more but less than 100 million yuan, shall be charged a monthly donation of 2/1000. Grade C, with a current value of less than 50 million yuan, shall be charged a monthly donation of 1/1000.

Xu Yongzuo Reports That Landlords Cannot Afford It

Based on the above donation rate, Xu Yongzuo has a numerical report. He used the rent of the 26th year as a standard and divided it into three grades, A, B, and C. He explained that if the municipal construction surtax is borne by the landlords, the landlords will suffer unbearable losses. Assuming that Grade A houses had a monthly rent of 500 yuan in the 26th year, calculated at the statutory 160 times, the current rent is 80,000 yuan. After deducting the 20% housing tax of 16,000 yuan, the net income is 64,000 yuan. The value of this type of house in the 26th year was 50,000 yuan. Calculated at 5,000 times, the current value is 250 million yuan. The municipal construction surtax of 3/1000 is 750,000 yuan. In addition to the net income of 64,000 yuan in rent, he will lose 686,000 yuan. Even if the landlord and tenant each bear half, he will still lose 311,000 yuan. For Grade B houses, assuming that the pre-war rent was 100 yuan and the current rent is 16,000 yuan, after deducting the 3,200 yuan housing tax, the net income is 12,800 yuan. The current value is 50 million yuan, and the municipal construction surtax of 2/1000 needs to be paid, which is 100,000 yuan, so he will lose 87,200 yuan. If the landlord and tenant bear the average, the landlord will also lose 27,200 yuan. For Grade C houses, assuming that the pre-war rent was 20 yuan and the current statutory rent is 3,200 yuan, after deducting the housing tax of 640 yuan, the net income is 2,560 yuan. The current value is about 10 million yuan, and the municipal construction surtax of 10,000 yuan should be paid, so he will lose 7,440 yuan. If the landlord and tenant bear the average, the landlord will also lose 2,440 yuan. Finally, Xu Yongzuo asked: "Is this method reasonable, is it possible? As a result, the landlord has to give up the house, because having a house not only does not make money, but also loses money. Who wants a house? In the autumn of such a serious housing shortage, it is also impossible in fact. Moreover, if the municipal construction surtax is paid by the landlord, it becomes a property tax, which is unreasonable. In name and in fact, it should be paid by those who enjoy municipal construction."

Speaker Pan's on Collection Methods

Speaker Pan discovered a very strange thing. He said: "At present, it is very difficult to assess the value of houses, and the appraisers of the Finance Bureau can manipulate the power, which inevitably leads to abuses. The municipal construction donations are collected according to the current value of the house. Councilor Xu Yongzuo has already provided a numerical explanation. I have also calculated it slightly. However, the result I have calculated is about higher than that of Councilor Xu. It is estimated that Grade C houses should pay a municipal construction donation of 12,000 yuan, Grade B should pay 120,000 yuan, and Grade A should pay 800,000 yuan. But there is one thing that is very strange. If the housing tax is paid according to the No. 2 method, the city government can collect 18 billion yuan in half a year, which is enough to make up for the budget deficit. But the burden on the tenants has been reduced. I don't know how the Finance Bureau assessed it, but this method is beneficial to the general people. We have already decided that the housing tax should be collected at 20% of the actual rent. Now we can adopt the method of No. 2, but not the housing tax, but the municipal construction surtax. According to the method of No. 2, this autumn, the housing tax for Grade A houses is three times higher than in summer, the housing tax for Grade B houses is two times higher than in summer, and the housing tax for Grade C houses is one time higher than in summer. Another loan will be added in winter. The so-called summer housing tax collection method is to collect 14% of the 560 times the rent in the 26th year. That is to say, for Grade C houses, the rent in the 26th year was 20 yuan, the summer housing tax is 1,512 yuan, the autumn is 3,024 yuan, and the winter is 6,048 yuan. In the autumn and winter seasons, the average is only more than 4,500 yuan, and the housing tax of 20% of the actual rent paid by the landlord can also be deducted. But according to the municipal construction surtax donation rate, drawing 1/1000 of the current value of the house means that if the tenant bears the average, he also has to pay a municipal construction surtax of 5,000 yuan. So, according to this method, tenants are cheaper. According to this method, for Grade B houses that rented for 100 yuan before the war, 22,680 yuan will be paid in autumn and 45,360 yuan will be paid in winter. But according to the municipal construction surtax donation rate, if the tenant bears half, he also has to pay 50,000 yuan. For Grade A houses that rented for 500 yuan before the war, 151,200 yuan will be paid in autumn and 302,400 yuan will be paid in winter. But according to the municipal construction surtax donation rate, if the tenant bears half, he also has to pay 375,000 yuan. Therefore, if the collection is carried out according to the method of No. 2, and the housing tax that the landlord should pay is deducted from the total amount, the tenant can get a lot cheaper. According to this number, no matter what grade of houses are, the money paid by the tenants is less than half of the municipal construction surtax drawn according to the current value of the house. Therefore, I suggest adopting this method." All the councilors applauded and agreed enthusiastically.

Burden Issue: A Debate

Director Gu and Lu Shidao also gave explanations regarding the numerical statistics. What Director Gu explained was that after the housing tax is collected at 20% of the actual rent, the burden on the landlord depends on the rent he receives. The higher the rent, the higher the housing tax will be. What Lu Shidao explained was that it is unreasonable for the municipal construction surtax to be borne by the landlord.

Traditional first looked at it from a theoretical perspective. He said: "I don't calculate numbers, but we want to pursue the truth. To be honest, neither the landlord nor the tenant can afford the burden. What is being collected now is the municipal construction surtax. Whoever enjoys the municipal construction has to pay the donation. If the name is not correct, the words are not reasonable. We have to understand this point. As for the landlord, he will have to pay land value tax and land appreciation tax in the future, and that number will certainly be very large." Xi Yushu also spoke in pursuit of the truth, believing that the truth is that the municipal construction surtax should be borne by the tenant. Deputy Speaker Xu said: "Brothers are laborers but speak for capitalists. What the rich people have in their hands now is definitely not real estate, but gold bars, US dollars, cotton yarn and other goods. Taxes should be reasonable." The final conclusion was also that "the municipal construction surtax should be borne by those who enjoy municipal construction."

Zhang Zhihan once stood up and shouted, please the councilors, don't think too much about the landlord and forget the residents. You must know that the residents cannot afford it either. Wang Jian'e also insisted that the burden on the tenants should be taken into account.

Don't Forget the Sublessee

Regarding the estimation method of the current value of the house, Li Wenjie, Jin Runxiang, Tao Baichuan and others all expressed many opinions. Feng Youzhen reminded everyone not to forget the third type of people besides the landlord and the tenant: the sublessee. Because to the head landlord, he is a tenant; to the subtenant, he is a landlord, and he always has the upper hand and takes all the advantages. So we must never relax the sublessee.

The councilors argued endlessly. But in the end, Speaker Pan stood up and spoke, finally obtaining the approval of an absolute majority and resolving the motion.

(Photo by Our Newspaper)

Page 5

Enemy Nationals Attempt to Restrict Freedom of Speech: A Case Closely Watched by Chinese and Foreign Journalists: Trial of American Reporter Concluded, Lawyers on Both Sides Deliver Eloquent Arguments, Court Orders Sentencing on the 27th

[Our Report] The District Court continued the trial of the case in which German Nazi suspect Shen Ke sued Rundall, the director of the Shanghai office of the American United Press, for defamation at 3:00 PM yesterday. The audience was packed, with Americans making up nearly half of it. Shen Ke did not appear and was represented by his agent, lawyer Yao Zhaodi. Rundall was defended by lawyer Chen Tingrui. The lawyers on both sides engaged in a fierce debate. At 4:30 PM, the court announced the end of the debate and scheduled sentencing for 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 27th. According to Mr. Chen Tingrui, although the court has scheduled sentencing, it does not necessarily mean that it will accept the case.

The trial began in an extremely tense atmosphere. When Rundall stepped into the defendant's box, he appeared slightly uneasy. Yuan Lunren, a reporter from the United Press, stood beside him, translating everyone's statements in a very low voice. Lawyer Yao first stated to the court that Shen Ke could not attend because he was detained in the guardhouse of the American Military Court. The court then approved Yao's representation.

From the Perspective of International Law, Shen Ke Has No Right to Sue

Lawyer Chen Tingrui then stood up and defended Rundall in a slow but forceful tone. He said: "According to the law, the court should not accept cases that are prosecuted without a self-accusation. Shen Ke is not allowed to file a self-accusation based on international law and the law of the Republic of China. According to international law, Shen Ke is a German national and a well-known Nazi member, listed on our country's list of those to be sent back to Germany, and is still detained in the American Military Court for war crimes. China and Germany have not yet made peace and are still legally at war. Therefore, the plaintiff's identity is that of an enemy national. Whether enemy nationals have the right to sue is not explicitly stipulated in our country's laws. However, international law is a law commonly recognized by international society, so international law should be regarded as part of the laws of each country. According to the provisions of international law after World War I, there is a relative recognition of the right of enemy nationals to sue. The United Kingdom and the United States recognize the right of enemy nationals to sue, but there is a prerequisite, that is, the enemy national must continue to reside in the host country and be a law-abiding citizen, allowed to reside by the local government. Shen Ke has not been allowed by our government to continue to reside in China. The Shanghai Office of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs has sent a letter proving that 'Shen Ke is one of the German nationals on the list to be sent back to Germany and has been detained for suspected war crimes.' Mr. Chen presented the letter and continued, saying, 'This proves that Shen Ke is definitely not welcomed or allowed to reside in our country by the government. Moreover, Shen Ke is not only a Nazi member, but also a spy among the Nazis! Therefore, from the perspective of international law, Shen Ke has no right to sue.'"

According to the Provisional Constitution, Please Do Not Accept the Case

Secondly, regarding our country's Provisional Constitution, according to Article 15 of Chapter 2 of the Provisional Constitution, the people have the freedom of speech and publication. Our government has also repeatedly proclaimed freedom of speech as a political program. The defendant is the director of the China office of the American United Press. As a journalist, his freedom of speech should be even more strictly protected by law. Articles 19 and 7 of the Publication Law have provisions for this. Journalists report news with the aim of recording everything they hear. Today, the plaintiff, as a Nazi enemy national, attempts to restrict the freedom of friendly people and sue the court, which is insane! It must be known that Nazi law can prohibit the people's freedom of speech, but Nazi law cannot be applied in democratic China! This case is not only related to journalists and publishers from friendly countries in China, but also of great importance to domestic journalists and publishers. The court should not accept it.

Mr. Chen then quoted the writings of international law authority Oppenheim, stating that enemy nationals cannot file lawsuits nor appear in court for defense. He also quoted Noyes, saying that the protection of foreigners should be limited to those who are law-abiding and continue to reside. He also said that this case has attracted international attention. The English-language Shanghai Evening Post & Mercury published a dispatch from New York saying that the verdict of this case will greatly affect whether foreign journalists have the opportunity to have freedom of speech in China. For the sake of maintaining freedom of speech, the Chinese government should not accept this case, etc. It is said that today, representing the defendant, based on international law and the law, he requests the court to issue a ruling not to accept the case.

Plaintiff's Agent States: Private Rights Should Be Protected Regardless of Victory or Defeat

Shen Ke's agent, lawyer Yao Zhaodi, then stood up and replied, stating: "The defendant's lawyer's defense is based on international law and the law. Now, let us first respond to the law aspect. The law does stipulate freedom of speech, but this freedom should have considerable restrictions, otherwise the chapter on defamation in the criminal law could be abolished. Therefore, the so-called freedom should be freedom within the scope of the law. Whether the defendant has exceeded the freedom of speech stipulated by the law, please investigate and make a verdict of guilty or not guilty. Secondly, regarding international law, in feudal times, when wars occurred, the defeated had no other way but to become slaves. However, it should be known that this kind of concept is a concept of feudal times. The books presented by the defendant's lawyer have not been read by this seat. Whether they are out of context cannot be said, but at most, they are just one person's opinion and cannot be taken as evidence. Regardless of victory or defeat, the private rights of the people should be protected. In 1907, various countries signed an international convention in The Hague, with countries such as China, the United States, and Germany signing on it. Among them, Article 23, Paragraph 8 of Chapter 4 clearly stipulates that it is specifically prohibited to eliminate the right of the people of the defeated country to sue, etc. Because people cannot live without their rights and cannot be without the protection of the law. To give an example, rape cases are those that can only be prosecuted if the victim is a German national, and if they are not allowed to sue, then this case will not be established!"

The defendant's actions have actually exceeded the scope that a journalist should adhere to. The source of the news he released is unclear, and there are many exaggerations. His actions have harmed our country's public order. After this case occurred, Rundall even appealed to the US State Department, intending to use the political power of his own country to coerce our government! Please, the court, consider the case, consider the facts, be calm and peaceful, and discuss the case on the merits.

Shen Ke's being sent back to his country is a "general" evacuation of foreigners. Those who are sent away are not necessarily bad elements. Our government is only afraid that they will not be able to maintain their lives after staying in China, so they are ordering them back to their country. Therefore, the point that the defendant's lawyer says that those who are sent away are the scum is not worth adopting. Although Shen Ke has now been prosecuted, he has not yet been convicted. The crimes charged by the American Military Court are only spying on military intelligence, which is actually without any factual basis. They actually want to fabricate crimes and deliberately create a big prison!"

At this time, Lawyer Chen angrily stood up and said that the prosecution of this case is illegal, and the defendant's side does not want to follow this illegal path and discuss the substance of this case.

There are Three So-Called Pieces of Evidence

However, despite this attack, Lawyer Yao continued his statement, saying that the defendant could not prove that the facts he defamed were true and reliable, and the plaintiff's side could prove that Rundall's words were not facts at all. There are three pieces of evidence: (1) Ambassador Chen Jie has a letter proving that Shen Ke's actions have always been beneficial to China. (2) Shen Ke left Chongqing on July 11, 1941, via Hanoi to Shanghai, which can be proven by the endorsements on his passport. When he left Chongqing, China had not yet declared war on Germany, but Rundall now says that his departure from Chongqing was to sabotage our country's underground work, which is clearly fabricated. (3) After Shen Ke returned to Shanghai, he often interacted with important people in charge of our country's underground work. Wu Shaoshu has a letter proving that he and Shen Ke often met due to the introduction of the person in charge of the Organization Department and called Shen Ke a loyal friend of China. When he was in Chongqing, he often praised our country's resistance to Japan in his reports and revealed that Germany had pro-Japanese tendencies. Wu's certificate also stated, "We often meet, but there is no mutual utilization or exchange of information." He also said, "I have always trusted Shen Ke without any doubt, so I often meet with him," and later stated, "My acquaintance with Shen Ke and the relationship that developed afterward have all been reported to the Organization Department for the record." It can be seen that what Rundall wrote is pure fabrication.

Lawyer Chen then rose again to reply, in addition to reiterating that Shen Ke's self-accusation was illegal, and said: "The Nazis have long since abandoned international law and treaties. The agent for the self-accusation considers Oppenheim's writings to be 'one person's opinion,' but no matter how brilliant the agent's research on international law is, it is probably not as good as this authority. There are different theories on the degree of binding of the Hague Convention. Whether it is applicable should be determined by each country's government. Taking the United Kingdom and Germany as an example, they have long expressed that they do not recognize it. The binding of treaties should be based on reciprocal treatment. Germany itself has already stopped applying it, so why seek public protection now?"

Why Not Attend? Why Detention?

As for the statement that the defendant attempted to use political power to coerce China, that is even more ridiculous! It concerns the international problem between the three countries of China, the United States, and Germany. The defendant is not wrong to observe his own government and has not attempted to use political power at all! The plaintiff should know that he has a guilty conscience, because he actually wants to use the power of the Chinese court's verdict to try to overturn the evidence presented by the American Military Court.

The agent for the self-accusation says that enemy nationals who are sent back are not necessarily bad guys, which also lacks common sense. The Chinese government's evacuation of enemy nationals does not have a fixed standard. Those evacuated by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs are Nazi elements, spies, and hooligans. If the two thousand German foreigners who were left in China were to sue here today, this lawyer would not object. Also, let me ask whether the overseas Chinese in Germany sued Germany during the war between China and Germany? Only if you can prove that you have the right to sue can you talk about reciprocity. Moreover, the release of this news was not limited to the United Press. The Associated Press has it, as well as the Shen Bao and the Xin Wen Bao. The source of the news is actually the press conference of the American military headquarters. Finally, there is one more point: According to our country's criminal procedure law, if the self-accuser does not attend after being summoned without a valid reason, the case should not be accepted. The self-accuser in this case has been summoned twice. Why didn't he attend? If it is said that it is because he is being detained, then why is he being detained? Can this be considered a valid reason? Please consider this, Court."

Rundall then began to speak after standing for an hour and a half, saying that he completely agreed with his defender's argument and did not want to prove whether Shen Ke was a spy today. The source of his report was the US military, and the agent for the self-accusation today seems to want me to prove whether the words of the US military authorities are accurate.

At 4:30, the court declared the end of the debate and scheduled sentencing for 2:00 PM on the afternoon of the 27th.

Electric Heaters Banned This Winter to Reduce Electricity Load

[Our Report] Winter is coming soon. In addition to actively preparing winter clothing, you must also be thinking about how to keep your bedroom and living room warm in the cold. Undoubtedly, installing an electric heater is the most ideal, economical, and convenient. However, this year is different from previous years. The electricity demand in the city has already exceeded the electricity production. Electricity for factories is still being cut off in shifts, let alone the extravagant electric heating. In order to maintain normal power supply, Mayor Wu has decided not to allow electric heaters this year. The power company will dismantle the electric heating devices of users throughout the city. Direct supply of current to electric stoves will remain the same. If the Shanghai Electric Power Company removes the extra burden of electric heaters, then electricity for lighting and electric stoves (limited to those formally equipped with electric stove meters) can be supplied adequately, and there is no need to worry about the power problem in winter.
