Broad Daylight Robbery in the Downtown Area: Daring to Resist Arrest and Open Fire: Asia Money Exchange Suffers Heavy Losses

[Our Report] Yesterday was the first anniversary of the opening of the Asia Money Exchange at No. 818 North Sichuan Road. Business was booming due to the sharp rise in gold and US dollars in recent days. Suddenly, at 1:00 PM, a robber dressed in a navy blue suit, carrying a briefcase, claimed that he wanted to buy a large gold bar. A clerk invited him to the inner room. While looking at the goods, the robber opened the briefcase, pulled out two automatic weapons, and forced all personnel not to make a sound. At that time, five other robbers, each armed with guns, followed in. One robber acted as a lookout, sitting on the counter outside the room, pretending to be a staff member. One robber guarded the back door, one robbed, and two guarded the clerks. While the robbery was in progress, a Russian man came to sell US dollars and was driven into the inner room by the lookout, who ordered the Russian man to "sit down" in English. The robbers looted more than one hundred taels of gold, more than eight million in cash, and two thousand five hundred US dollars, putting them all into a travel bag. At the time, the lookout was heard shouting, "The wind is coming!" and they fled north through the front door. During the robbery, a Zhou surname employee of the exchange took the opportunity to slip out through the back door and reported to the nearby police. When the robbers carried the stolen goods out of the store, the police shot at them. The robbers also returned fire and resisted arrest. Because the location was crowded, the robbers were able to escape. After learning of the incident, Director Xuan ordered the Hongkou Police Branch to solve the case as soon as possible, since the robbers dared to rob in broad daylight.

Breakthrough in Air Trafficking Case Involving Twists and Turns; Large Scale; Agencies Established in Major Cities Including Beiping, Tianjin, Shanghai, and Taiwan; Thirteen Men and Women to Be Sent to the District Prosecutor's Office Today

[Report from Our Newspaper] The air trafficking case recently cracked in this city has resulted in the arrest of over twenty suspects. After several days of investigation by the police bureau, apart from a portion who were released on bail due to insufficient evidence, the remaining thirteen suspects (including one female) have all been interrogated. Today, they will be transferred to the District Prosecutor's Office along with confiscated morphine gold bars valued at approximately one hundred million yuan, and specially made suitcases with hidden compartments used for drug transportation. The case's breakthrough involved many twists and turns. The Criminal Police Division of the Police Bureau mobilized officers from the Second Section, working day and night to pursue clues, even expanding the police network to Beiping, Tianjin, Taiwan, and other places. Ultimately, all suspects were apprehended.

The incident began on the 10th of this month when Director Xuan received a confidential report stating that a major drug trafficker, Song Zhi'an, residing at No. 32, Hehefang, Lin Sen Middle Road, had recently entrusted a large sum of money to the Xinhua Bank in this city for remittance to Tianjin. This money was said to be used for purchasing and transporting morphine. Director Xuan immediately instructed Chief Zhang of the Criminal Division that night to dispatch officers for investigation. After Chief Zhang discussed the matter with Section Chief of the Second Section, he immediately dispatched officers Feng Qishan and clerk Li Xiqing to Hehefang for investigation that night. Unexpectedly, the location turned out to be an empty house, and the homeowner, Zhu Qishan, had also escaped when arrested by the District Prosecutor's Office in a drug trafficking case ten days earlier. As the situation seemed suspicious, Feng and others conducted a search and obtained a house contract for Zhu Qishan, showing that he had taken over a house at No. 10, Pan Neng Street. They followed up on the investigation and, by the afternoon of the 11th, learned of Zhu Qishan's hidden address. They then led police officers Zhang Yunming, Ding Zhaogan, Gao Fuhai, Ding Wenjiang, and others to Room 12, No. 4, Kunshan Garden, where they arrested Zhu in a suite. Two pounds of caffeine and half a washbasin of black drug material were confiscated on the spot. During the search, a Taiwanese man named Sun Zhicheng arrived, carrying four gold bars weighing 39 taels, 5 mace, and 4 fen, intending to purchase morphine. He was immediately detained, and officers were dispatched to his residence at No. 9, Jishan Lane, Wuchang Road, where three pounds and two taels of morphine raw material and a pistol were confiscated. At that time, a well-dressed, robust man from Hebei arrived with an officer. The officer carried a suitcase. Upon entering the room and realizing the unusual situation, he attempted to flee, but was stopped by the officers. After questioning, one was identified as Zhang Mingyuan, 32 years old, and the other claimed to be Yan Dongfu, 37 years old, an upper-colonel officer of the 94th Army, claiming to have arrived in Shanghai from Tianjin on a China National Aviation Corporation (CNAC) plane. When the officers asked them to produce identification, they hesitated, confirming that they were impersonating officers. The suitcase was opened and searched, revealing three pounds and five taels of morphine raw material in the hidden compartment of the suitcase. At this point, in addition to taking all the above-mentioned suspects to the bureau, officers were stationed at the location day and night. Simultaneously, the Hongkou Police Branch also received a confidential report and arrested five accomplices in the case at No. 54, Yifuli, Baoshan Road, and Room 311 of the Royal Hotel, including Taiwanese nationals Li Hongying, Zhang Gentian, Zhang Yiren, Li Dingguo, and Zhang Li Bingkun (female). Details have already been reported in this newspaper. Later, during the investigation, the police bureau learned that the main agency of the case was located in Beiping, Tianjin, Taiwan, and other places, and the key person in charge was Song Zhi'an. A telegram was sent to the Tianjin Police Bureau for assistance, and he was arrested on the 15th of this month. In Shanghai, four more suspects, Zhou Da, Ma Baiwu, Lü Xinquan, and Song Zixin, were successively arrested, and three specially made suitcases with hidden compartments, thirty-five rubber sheaths for concealing morphine, payment slips for drug trafficking profits, and drafts of round-trip telegrams were confiscated. A Northeast Advance Army identification card and a Northeast Advance Army military certificate were also found at Zhou Da's residence.

Do Not Hope to Use the Blood and Sweat of Countless Citizens to Adorn Unnecessary Educational Facades

City Councilors Shen Ding and Others Propose Abolishing Art Normal Schools, etc.

[Report from Our Newspaper] City councilors Shen Ding, Jiang Huaishu, Lu YinChu, He Yuanming, etc., will present a temporary motion on the last day of the postponed City Council meeting today (the 24th), proposing that the City Government order the City Education Bureau to promptly adjust subordinate institutions, save expenditures, and popularize national education. Their reasons are as follows: The City Education Bureau's policy report to the Provisional City Council and the City Government's proposed work plan (education section) for the 35th year both mention increasing vocational schools, but in practice, there has been no active preparation. However, institutions not included in the plan, such as Art Normal Schools, suddenly opened, which shows that the Education Bureau's so-called plan is nothing more than a paper document. Therefore, institutions that have already been established, such as the Experimental Drama School and various centers, may not necessarily consider their value to education in the current stage of the city. What the citizens directly feel as an urgent need is that there are too few municipal primary and secondary schools, and children do not have suitable places to study. The citizens do not hope that the city government will use the blood and sweat of countless people to decorate unnecessary educational facades. Therefore, several measures are proposed as follows, and public decision is requested: Measures (1) The Experimental Drama School, the Experimental Public School, etc., should be abolished immediately, and the remaining school buildings should be converted into national schools. (2) The Municipal Art Normal School should be abolished immediately, and the specialized normal school should be merged with other normal schools. (3) The Music Center, the Art Center, the Craft Center, and the Science Experimental Sub-Center should be entrusted to schools, institutions, and groups to be jointly operated, or abolished directly. They should not be independent institutions. (4) Other matters that should be delayed or can be merged should be investigated and merged separately. (5) All expenditures saved due to the abolishment and merger of unnecessary institutions should be used entirely to develop national education.

Wonderful Tactics Displayed Perfectly; Qunsheng Beats Dongfang Team Again

60 to 38, Almost Double the Score; Qunsheng Three Wins in Three Games, Veteran Submits

[Report from Our Newspaper] The Qunsheng Basketball Team played its third game against the Dongfang Team in Shanghai yesterday. Dongfang, with its disorganized crowd and lack of connection, fought hard, but Qunsheng made full use of its exquisite tactics. The Dongfang veterans were helpless, and as a result, Qunsheng won again by a large margin of 60 to 38. The first half was 30 to 20. With yesterday's call from Dongfang, the gymnasium was packed, far exceeding the previous two games, which was the first grand occasion for the visiting team in Shanghai.

Incredibly Wonderful

Qunsheng's performance yesterday was even better than the previous two games. Chen Jinde planned from the middle, using shielding methods. The two forwards were like butterflies flitting through flowers, competing beautifully in the high and low posts, which was truly wonderful. Cai Wenhua and Cai Wenzhang's ease and accuracy in shooting the basket were delightful, and the teamwork during the entire team's attack and the speed of the defense can be said to be fully displayed. No wonder Dongfang bowed its head and submitted. The team's spirit was also admirable. Yesterday, there were occasional performances of dissatisfaction with the referee. I hope that those who do will change it, and those who do not will work harder.

Taking the Lead from Beginning to End

Dongfang sent Ren Xiangcheng, Tang Baokun, Qin Xunze, Wang Nanzhen, and Liu Jingxing into the game. After the start of the game, Qunsheng's Cai Wenhua scored twice, first scoring two goals. Dongfang fought hard, and Liu Jingxing and Qin Xunze chased to 4 points each, then to 6 points each. After that, it was seen that Qunsheng used high-speed fast breaks, so the score gradually took the lead, and Dongfang followed the situation. The first half was 30 to 20, and Qunsheng won by 10 points.

In the second half, both sides made adjustments. Qunsheng replaced Cai Wenzhang with Cai Lianke, and Dongfang replaced Liu Jingxing with Zhang Shaoqing. Ren Xiangcheng scored first, but it was a flash in the pan. Qunsheng showed its power again, and Cai Wenhua's accurate shooting and follow-up under the basket gradually increased the score to 46 to 23. Dongfang frequently adjusted its new forces to respond to the enemy and used force to defeat the enemy. Qunsheng called up Zhang Yuyi and others. Dongfang tried to catch up and once made it 45 to 34. Qunsheng urgently used the ideal lineup, and the difference was seen again. Later, Yang Renhui committed five fouls, but before long, the whistle blew, and Qunsheng won with a score of 60 to 38, three wins in three games.

Notes on Completing the Household Reregistration Form (Continued)

Family members who specialize in household chores are classified as unemployed according to regulations. However, general surveys often list them as "personnel services." "Personnel services" refer to household management, servants, and hired labor that receive direct compensation. Managing one's own household cannot be confused with personnel services that receive direct compensation. For the sake of distinction, those who manage their own household should fill in "managing household affairs" to distinguish them from "personnel services" that receive compensation.

The categories of occupations are as follows: Concise Table of Occupational Classification Industry (1) Agriculture, (Explanation) All those engaged in the production of agriculture, forestry, fishery, animal husbandry, hunting, and logging belong to this category. (Examples) Farming, gardening, forestry, fishing, animal husbandry, hunting, logging, other agriculture.

(2) Mining, All those engaged in the exploitation of natural resources belong to this category. (Examples) Metal mining, non-metal mining, salt industry, coal industry, petroleum industry, earth and stone industry, other mining.

(3) Industry, All those engaged in manufacturing belong to this category. (Examples) Wood and stone manufacturing, daily necessities manufacturing, woodworking manufacturing, smelting industry, metal products industry, machinery manufacturing, transportation equipment manufacturing, national defense equipment manufacturing, construction industry, water and electricity industry, chemical industry, textile industry, leather, fur, bone, and rubber manufacturing, food and beverage manufacturing, paper and paper product manufacturing, printing industry, publishing industry, ornament, stationery, and instrument manufacturing, incense making industry (not exclusively for superstition), other industries.

(4) Commerce, All those engaged in the sale of materials and finance, or introduction for profit-making purposes, belong to this category. (Examples) Sales industry, brokerage and introduction industry, financial insurance industry, supplies of daily necessities, slaughtering industry, non-state-run banking industry, other commerce.

Refutation of Rumors of Foreign Exchange Readjustment The President of the Central Bank States that He Has Heard Nothing of the Sort Efforts are Being Made to Curb Capital Flight to Hong Kong

[Report from this newspaper] Mr. Bei Zuyi, the president of the Central Bank, told reporters of this newspaper yesterday: The rumors circulating in the market that foreign exchange will be readjusted again are purely unfounded. Regarding the rumors circulating in the capital that the relevant parties have drafted a foreign exchange adjustment method and plan to make frequent adjustments with small ratios, he said that he had not heard of anything of the sort. He also did not know what "relevant parties" the rumors were referring to. He said: In short, all the recent rumors in the market about foreign exchange are completely groundless. He did not want to comment too much in the newspaper, so as not to be used by speculators as material for selective interpretation.

Regarding the matter of capital flight to Hong Kong, he said that efforts are being made to find ways to control it. He ultimately hopes that the people can abide by the law more, which would be of great help.

The Central Bank will hold an administrative affairs meeting in the capital on Double Ten Day. He said: The meeting has not been held for a long time due to the impact of the war. Branches from all over the country will send personnel to participate in this meeting to pool ideas, exchange opinions, and study how to improve business operations so that the Central Bank can become the bank of banks. At the same time, they will discuss how to communicate the business of the head office and branches, as well as domestic exchange issues.

Central Bank Stipulates Measures for Deferred Foreign Exchange Delivery

In view of the recent large number of merchants applying to designated banks to defer the delivery of foreign exchange sold on a forward basis, the Central Bank yesterday sent a circular to all designated banks, detailing the following regulations regarding applications for deferred foreign exchange delivery:

(1) Merchants requesting to purchase foreign exchange, with the exception of those specified in Item 3, must have written documents proving the purpose of the foreign exchange purchased, and such documents must be approved by the designated bank. Designated banks should pay close attention to their own responsibilities when reviewing the above applications.

(2) For imported goods, with the exception of those specified in Items 3 and 4, there must be an irrevocable letter of credit or purchase order (Irrevocable L/C or A/P) guaranteeing payment, unless otherwise authorized by the Central Bank.

(3) The above regulations may be separately negotiated for long-established importers with established payment practices, and the required amount may be approved and allocated on a regular basis according to their needs.

(4) For import drafts collected by banks exceeding US$500 C.I.F. or its equivalent, designated banks must obtain the prior permission of the Central Bank before selling the foreign exchange.

(5) The points listed in this circular do not apply to import goods for which the regulations stipulated in Circular No. 26 of April 4 of this year are still valid.

(6) For foreign exchange sold on or after August 19, if it is not settled by the due date, the designated bank may cancel the settlement at the exchange rate on the day of the forward sale. The designated bank must resell the cancelled foreign exchange to the Central Bank at the original purchase price.

26 Designated Banks Handle it Themselves Replacements to be Redeemed Within One Month

[Report from this newspaper] The Securities Exchange stipulates that the margin for brokers is set at 50 million yuan for each of the bond and stock markets. The exchange has complied with this. At the same time, it has approved a letter from the Business Bureau of the Central Bank designating the banks of the Shanghai Banking Association, namely Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Zhejiang Xingye Bank, China & South Sea Bank, Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank, Jincheng Banking Corporation, The New China Trust & Savings Bank, China Land Bank, The Shanghai-Kuo Hua Commercial & Savings Bank, China Development Bank, The Chuyeh Bank, China United Bank, The Sze Ming Commercial Bank, The Chung Nan Bank, China Trade Development Corporation, The Continental Bank, China Enterprises Bank, China Industrial Bank, China National Products Bank, Kianghai Bank, Industrial and Mining Bank of China, China General Chamber of Commerce Bank, Chekiang Commercial Bank, Guangdong Development Bank, and National Trust & Savings Bank, a total of 26 banks, to handle the written guarantee matters for the replacement portion of the exchange's brokers. The exchange should send a letter to all brokers to check and contact the 26 designated banks by September 27 of this year to handle the matter. Obtain a written guarantee of 30 million yuan of national currency for each market with the exchange as the payee, and submit it to the Central Bank for collection. And wait for the exchange to notify you to redeem the above-mentioned written guarantee with replacements from the Central Bank within one month after the opening, in order to comply with the Ministry's order.

Apply for Reduction Rationing Price Increased

The Association's Notice Eight Measures

The following is an excerpt of the provisional measures decided by the meeting for yarn factories to open for sale cotton yarn:

1. Customers who purchase cotton yarn are temporarily limited to the original customers of each factory, and priority is given to applications from end users.

2. The above-mentioned end users who have a real need to purchase cotton yarn should first fill out an application form with the yarn factory they usually deal with, stating the count, quantity, purpose, and other items of the cotton yarn they intend to purchase. The amount of the application filled in by the customer must be limited to the actual needs. If there is speculation or false reporting, each factory may reduce or cancel its application qualification at its discretion.

3. After receiving and reviewing the purchase application form, each yarn factory will determine, based on past yarn purchase records, whether the applied quantity is accurate. If there is any inaccuracy, it should be corrected at any time and sent to the association for decision before 12:00 noon every day. Before 4:00 PM on the same day, the association will notify each yarn factory of the quantity and standard price (with 20-count cotton yarn as the standard) decided by the association, and forward it to the applicant. Each yarn factory and applicant may not increase or decrease the decided quantity and price on their own.

4. If there is a surplus of the amount of cotton yarn to be sold by each factory, the association will distribute it on behalf of the factory.

5. After receiving the notice, the applicant should sign a transaction contract with the factory on the same day and pay the full amount of the goods in cash on the next day.

6. When selling cotton yarn, each factory must ensure that each large package weighs 400 pounds net and each small package weighs 10 pounds net, and no small branches may be added separately.

7. The cotton yarn decided to be sold will be delivered as soon as possible, starting ten days after the date of payment.

8. If the applicant fails to fulfill the contract or make payment after receiving the decision notice, the association may cancel its application qualification.

The shipping companies also do not have a fixed amount for this item and must pay in advance before they can pick up the goods. In addition, when the cargo owner ships the goods from the warehouse within 10 days, he must pay a fee of 300 yuan per bag. Comparative Research on New and Old Income Taxes

— Xu Riqing

(3) Implementation of Comprehensive Income Tax

The previous classified income tax system in our country levied taxes based on income, such as profits from enterprises, interest from deposits, and rental income from houses. Therefore, it can be called an income tax. It failed to meet the principle of fair burden based on ability. Comprehensive income tax, however, taxes all income, so it is also known as general income tax. It uses the individual income of taxpayers as the calculation unit, so it is also called ad personam tax, that is, the total income of all kinds of income of each taxpayer is calculated, and then various expenses are deducted from the total income as the tax standard. For example, France implements comprehensive income tax, stipulating that all people in France with an annual income of more than 7,000 francs must pay this tax.

Article 3 of the new income tax law stipulates that in addition to the classified income tax levied in accordance with the preceding article, individuals whose total income exceeds 600,000 yuan shall be subject to a comprehensive income tax. The calculation method is to combine the individual's various incomes for the whole year into a total income, but the following items can be deducted: 1. 100,000 yuan per person for family members living together or relatives who must be supported; 2. 50,000 yuan per person for family members who are students in secondary schools or above; 3. Various income taxes and land taxes already paid (Article 19 of the same law). The method of declaration is that the obligated person shall report the type and amount of income of the previous year to the主管征收機關 (competent collection authority) before May 1 each year. The 主管征收機關 (competent collection authority) and the district and township offices or central primary schools establish a joint declaration association for review (Article 26 of the same law) to avoid the malpractice of false reports or non-reporting.

In the past, our country used the excuse of lax household registration and incomplete statistics to not implement the comprehensive income tax. This resolute decision to implement it this time is not without considerable reason. In the future, the collection of comprehensive income tax will be fraught with difficulties, which is inevitable. As the saying goes, "Human effort can overcome heaven," and it is expected that there will be a day to overcome these difficulties.

At the beginning of the establishment of the comprehensive income tax, people in the society and the public opinion circles feel that there is a suspicion of duplication. In fact, the classified income tax is a tax on income, and the comprehensive income tax is a tax on people, and there is no duplication, because the objects are different. The comprehensive income tax is most in line with the principle of ability to pay, and at the same time, the progressive tax system must adopt progressive tax rates. Our country's classified income tax is limited by the environment and insufficient conditions, and has failed to give full play to its effectiveness, so that those who have more pay more, and those who have less pay less. Taking the income from securities deposits as an example, both 10,000 yuan and 10,000,000 yuan of deposit income are subject to 10%, which is unreasonable. Therefore, the government adopts comprehensive income tax to make up for its deficiencies and prevent the concentration of wealth. The original intention of the legislation is perfect, and whether the implementation can be smooth remains to be seen the efforts of those in charge. Furthermore, considering the advanced countries, those who first levy classified income tax and then levy comprehensive income tax include France, the United Kingdom, and Italy. Moreover, the tax rates of comprehensive income tax in various countries are higher than those in our country. For example, the United States has a minimum tax rate of 13%, the United Kingdom has a tax rate of 10%, Japan has a tax rate of 10%, the United States has a maximum tax rate of 72%, the United Kingdom has a tax rate of 45%, Japan has a tax rate of 60%, while our country has a minimum tax rate (that is, those exceeding 600,000 yuan) of 5%, and a maximum tax rate of only 50%.

(4) A Major Prerequisite - Economic Stability

The newly promulgated income tax law this time has taken into account the actual situation and objective needs in terms of content, and is gradually moving towards a more reasonable path, which is encouraging. However, only four months have passed since the promulgation of the new income tax law. Due to the daily depreciation of the currency and the rising prices of goods, all clauses seem to have lost their timeliness. Taking only the starting point of the comprehensive income tax in the new income tax law as an example, it is already too low. It is reported that this starting point was based on the pre-war Shanghai living survey data and the retail price increase of 2,220 times in September of the 34th year of the Republic of China. According to the Shanghai 主要商品零售物價指數 (Main Commodity Retail Price Index) compiled by the Economic Research Department of the Central Bank, Shanghai's current prices have increased more than 3,700 times in June of this year. Now it is more than three months, plus the exchange rate adjustment, and prices have generally increased, estimated to be 4,000 times or even 10,000 times. In contrast, all suffer from the disease of being outdated. The other provisions, such as the tax exemption point for salary and remuneration income tax, are also the same. Therefore, all good laws and good intentions must be based on one major premise - economic stability - to be effective. (The End)

Travelogue in Northern Jiangsu (6) Blood Shadows on the Battlefield East of Taixian County

— Special Correspondent Hang Zhou

Taixian Dispatch, 10th of This Month

There are two long embankments in northern Jiangsu that are well known: on the left is the Grand Canal embankment, and on the right is the 范公堤 (Fan Gong Dyke). Between the embankments is a large area of lakes and marshes. In the past, people feared every year that floods would collapse the Grand Canal embankment, turning this area into a swamp. Since the Communist Party's army came to northern Jiangsu, people's fear of floods has been transferred. —— There are too many examples to prove that wherever the Communist army goes, it becomes a "sea of blood." —— "Sea of blood" is a more terrifying term than "flood"!

The topography of northern Jiangsu limits military activities, so the battles are fought either on the Grand Canal embankment or on the Fan Gong Dyke. When the Shaobo battle in late August was in full swing, the Communist army launched a sudden attack on the right flank, and battles broke out once again in places like Rugao, Haian, Qutang, and Huangqiao. The people who had just returned to their hometowns once again embarked on the road to destruction.

As a result, the focus of the war quickly shifted to the right. The Communist army's offensive was obviously not only echoing the left flank, but also attempting to further seize Liangtai and threaten Jiangnan. More than a month ago, the Communist army had made such an attempt and suffered a crushing defeat. Now it is reorganizing its forces, and the national army must of course crush it again.

Second Phase of the War Second Act

The situation on the right flank is dangerous, and the Communist army is very rampant. Taking Haian as an example, the Communist army used twelve regiments to surround the national army, which was only one-fifth of its size, but after fighting for more than a week, the Communist army could not move Haian even a little bit. Qutang and Daxiaobaimi have already fallen into the hands of the Communist army. The situation in Huangqiao was once unclear, and fighting is still going on nearby. In the bag-shaped area from Rugao to Baimi in the northwest and Huangqiao in the southwest, there are even more mobile Communist troops. Large and small battles are constantly taking place on the periphery of Taixian and Taixing counties.

The right flank is "lively," while the left flank appears silent. On September 6, the reporter boarded a "wild chicken" bus running on the Yangtai Road in Yangzhou to see the second act of the second phase of the war in northern Jiangsu.

The Yangtai Road is a major artery in northern Jiangsu at present. The national army has put in a lot of effort to open it up and maintain it. There are many fortresses on both sides of the road. These fortresses have all been stained with blood in front of them. Although they can no longer be seen now, I have seen one by one the smiles of the farmers who are harvesting the abundant rice crop in exchange for those bloodstains. This year is a great harvest year in northern Jiangsu. The Chinese farmers who "depend on the sky for food" should have thanked God, but in Gaoyou, Baoying... in those so-called "liberated areas," how many farmers are still shedding tears over their harvest!

Universal Vigor and Vitality Doing What One Says

After passing through checkpoints one after another, I arrived in Taixian. This is the reporter's second trip to Tai. Yangzhou is like a middle-aged woman, but Taixian is much younger. What I feel is universal vigor and vitality. County Magistrate Ding Zuobin is a graduate of the 16th class of the military academy and has served as a guerrilla commander. He is a complete soldier. The district chiefs, township chiefs, militia captains, and even the secretaries and section chiefs in the county government all have relationships with the military academy and guerrilla warfare. They have shared hardships and are now facing hardships. They usually joke around, but when they get down to business, they are really energetic and quick. Among the counties controlled by the national army in northern Jiangsu, Taixian can be said to be the one that cooperates with the military the most. Repairing roads and building fortifications are done as soon as they are said. Ding Zuobin cannot sit idly in the county government office for three days. He likes to run around and see everything. Some things require four or five official documents to be transferred and put on hold for ten days and eight days. He goes to the countryside himself and solves them with a single sentence.

The soldiers now are not all roughnecks, and some have quite good political cultivation. Ding Zuobin has the straightforward and enthusiastic personality of a northerner. The people of Taixian are proud to have such a county magistrate. He said that he doesn't know how to be an official, he only knows how to do things. He scolds his subordinates "not to spoil his affairs."

Jiangnan is a land of fish and rice, while Jiangbei is a land of salt and rice. They are both equally rich. If Jiangnan and Jiangbei have different sentiments, the most obvious may be in terms of the people's character: Jiangnan is weaker, while Jiangbei is quite strong. Strong people with organization are a very good local armed force. The general feeling in northern Jiangsu is that the local armed forces are not enough, but Taixian has silently made quite a bit of progress. Every township has a militia, with more than 2,000 people and more than 1,000 guns, helping the army a lot.

In the past two days, Dasizhuang, which is more than 20 miles southeast of Taixian and 18 miles away from the Kou-Tai Highway, was attacked by the Communist army. There were no national troops stationed there, and the militia resisted on its own, not allowing the Communist army to take advantage of it. Ding Zuobin received the report and personally led four or five hundred militiamen to reinforce it, driving the Communist army away in one fell swoop.

Jiangyan Approaching the Front Line Listening to Machine Gun Fire

On September 7, the reporter, accompanied by Wu Xiaode, Chief of Staff of the 108th Brigade, and Staff Officer Gao Hongsheng, inspected the eastern battlefield of Taixian, and Ding Zuobin also went along.

Starting early in the morning, we first went to Jiangyan. On the Tai-Jiang Road, commercial vehicles were nowhere to be seen, and military vehicles rushed around, quickly covering 36 miles. Jiangyan is a large town and a distribution center for grain. In previous years, the grain transport ships that stopped here were connected for three or four miles. It is only ten miles away from Magou, the front line here, and the sound of machine guns can be heard clearly every night. Having gotten used to it, no one is disturbed by it. A bathhouse is still painting its facade and choosing a lucky day to open. We didn't stay long and rushed to Magou.

In the sense of defending Taixian, Magou is a very important stronghold. Since the Communist army launched its offensive, it has cut off the Tai-Hai Road. On the evening of August 29, it gathered more than two regiments and took advantage of the fact that the national army had just changed its defenses, and rushed straight to Magou, hoping to take it in one fell swoop, coerce Jiangyan, and threaten Taixian. The garrison in Magou only had one company, but this company was not flustered at all. "Fighting doesn't depend on having a lot of people," they calmly guarded the fortifications, killing one when it came, and killing two together. The Communist army surrounded Magou and charged again and again, and those who came up could not go back. Company Commander Zheng Yadong listened to the Communist army's charge horn in the trench. It blew a total of 20 times, indicating that the 19 charges had all failed, and the 20th charge could not avoid its final fate, and they also fell down. The dark night passed away in the battle, and the sound of gunfire on the other side died down. The brothers jumped out of the trenches to greet the rays of the sun and took a look: "Ah! So many corpses!" They were so excited that they forgot their fatigue and counted them. There were three or four hundred bodies.

As soon as I arrived in Magou, the brothers of Zheng Yadong's company scrambled to tell me about this wonderful battle. I deliberately spoiled their fun and asked:

"How many casualties did you have?"

"One dead and four wounded," a soldier replied triumphantly.

One to four hundred, or five to two thousand (the total number of Communist army casualties), this record must make the Communist army gnash their teeth.

Sure enough, the impetuous Communist army came to "avenge" every night after that, but every night they brought corpses as gifts.

We once stood on a fortress to observe the terrain. I asked Battalion Commander Zhao Haiyun:

"How far is this from the Communist army's outpost?"

"Half a mile at most."

"Isn't it dangerous?" I asked in a very bookish tone.

"They dare not - the Communist army comes out at night."

Parachutes Ejected Supplying the Garrison

Back in Jiangyan, it was 3 p.m. After resting for a while, when we were preparing to return to Taixian, a bomber flew over the sky, slowly circling, seemingly looking for a target. Having seen too many planes, we paid no attention to it, when suddenly cries of alarm erupted from all around: "Dropping bombs!" People were shouting and running. I was also taken aback. Looking up, I saw several parachutes floating in the sky, swaying as they descended. "Not like bombs," I thought intuitively: "Bombs shouldn't be dropped here." But if it's not a bomb, it shouldn't be dropped here either. I thought again: "The plane must have mistaken the place."

The things that fell from the parachutes did not explode. "The plane probably mistook Jiangyan for Haian. The besieged garrison in Haian needs supplies." I thought further.

However, the plane did not realize its mistake, and it continued to eject parachutes one by one like a lotus flower. The villagers had never seen this thing before and rushed to the fields to search for it. Wu Zhifen, the commander of the 324th Regiment, ordered all the dropped items to be concentrated at the regimental headquarters for disposal.

At dusk, we returned to Taixian. The brigade contacted the air force and confirmed that the batch of things was to supply the garrison in Haian.

Although the siege of Haian has not been completely lifted, and the Communist troops in other places are still harassing everywhere, the dangerous period for northern Jiangsu has passed after the national army's redeployment. The army and people of northern Jiangsu have faith. "Where did the New Fourth Army come from? Beat it back where it came from!" A wild child adapted a song and sang. The Mid-Autumn Festival is coming! "The round moon shines on Kyushu, some families are happy and some are sad?" The food shops in Taixian started preparing two days ago to celebrate this poetic and picturesque festival, but the refugees who have no home to return to, sadly facing the bright moon, don't know how much new sorrow has been added!

A Fortress in Magou (Special Correspondent Hang Zhou)

Medical and Health

(1) Stomach Pain After Meals

Xia Nanxun asks: I have long suffered from stomach problems. When it occurs, I cannot move, sit, or lie down. My hands and feet are cold, and my stomach is cramping. I take about three teaspoons of "calcium magnesium" and it gets better immediately. In recent months, I have not wanted to eat in the morning, and I am not used to eating porridge. A few minutes after eating, my umbilical abdomen becomes so painful that I cannot bear it. I urgently want to defecate, which is clear, yellow, and hot. Please tell me: (1) What disease is abdominal distension and pain after meals? Is it related to stomach problems? (2) What special medicines can be used for emergency relief? (3) How can stomach problems be cured completely? Please show me the treatment method. (4) How should I adjust my diet? Is it appropriate to eat raw eggs in the morning? How should I take them?

[Answer from Dr. Gu Yuqi] (1) I am afraid that there is excessive stomach acid, colic, or even stomach ulcer symptoms. (2) Calcium magnesium can be tried. (3) It is best to go to the hospital for a detailed examination. (4) The diet should avoid sweet, sour, spicy, fruits, cold food, and cakes, 餅, cookies, and fried food. (5) Light milk or milk powder can be taken, and stewed eggs can be eaten. Eat more alkaline foods.

The Appeal of the Wuxi Knitting Industry

Editor: The industry of Wuxi City has always been known for its development, and it is called "Little Shanghai". The knitting industry in Wuxi also had a glorious history in the past, but since the victory, it has declined due to the dumping of foreign goods. Especially due to the lack of working capital, it has had to borrow high-interest loans, and has fallen into a difficult struggle. The government should promptly allocate industrial loans to alleviate the difficulties. Recently, I read in the newspaper that the Shanghai Branch of the China Production Promotion Association has organized an industrial loan syndicate to help small and medium-sized factories. I hope that it can be realized as soon as possible, and that the scope of loans can be expanded and handled fairly, so as to be in line with the actual situation and be widely available. In addition, the China Textile Corporation has always provided yarn, but it has not yet sold yarn to the knitting industry in Wuxi City, which uses the most yarn. I hope that it will be implemented quickly to reduce costs and compete for the market. (Wuxi County Knitting Industry Association)

Be Careful When Buying Fake Quinine Pills

To the Shen Bao 館 (Shen Bao Newspaper Office) and the Health Departments of all provinces of the Central Health Administration: This year, Shuangtao Quinine Pills are very expensive. General speculators only know how to seek profit and do not care about the lives of patients. They openly manufacture and sell fake pills to make profits. Some of them do not meet the standards, and some are entirely powdered and contain no quinine at all. General informal pharmacies, general goods shops, and drug stores in the interior purchase from vendors and sell them at the price of genuine brands. The ignorant rural people cannot distinguish between the genuine and the fake, and purchase and take them, but they are ineffective, so that the genuine products also lose their credibility. Such sales and manufacture of fake drugs harms patients, delays lives, and is a crime that cannot be forgiven. I especially ask your department to strictly order your subordinates to earnestly investigate and arrest them, so as to warn evil people and emphasize hygiene. I am very fortunate! (Doctor Yu Rubing)

Use Vacant Land to Build Vegetable Markets

At the intersection of Dihua Middle Road and Wuyuan Road in western Shanghai, there are vegetable stalls along the road, and the entry and exit of vehicles is very inconvenient. In recent years, the population has been large, and residents are overcrowded when buying vegetables. In addition, it is a major thoroughfare, and cars often have dangerous incidents. Residents are quite wary when traveling to and from. I think it is better to build a temporary vegetable market on the large open space at the intersection of Linsen Road and Fuxing West Road in the east, made of planks, like the style of the Nanshi South District Street. This equipment does not cost much, and stall rental fees can be collected. Moreover, the land has been vacant for a long time, which can avoid the accumulation of garbage and benefit hygiene. It is reported that the land was once owned by the enemy and puppets, so I respectfully suggest to the authorities that if it can be adopted, it will be beneficial to traffic safety and public hygiene. (Wang Shaofu)

Property Registration Certificate Fee is Too High

The Shanghai County Government, in order to facilitate collection, is handling transfer registration because the county was occupied for eight years and the land property was either sold or transferred. Our office belongs to the county, and because it is separated by the Huangpu River, it is very inconvenient to travel back and forth (the county government is in Minhang, west of the Huangpu River, while Districts 4 and 5 are east of the Huangpu River). A special commissioner was sent to the district office to handle it, saving the villagers the trouble of traveling back and forth, which is a good intention. However, the handling fee is as high as 6,800 yuan per mu. A house is counted as one mu, and a house in a city or town is counted as two mu. The high price is really unexpected. It is said that Chuansha County only charges 500 yuan per mu, why is there a difference of more than ten times? (Hu Zhifu of Chenxing Town)

Suxian Letters Take Nine Days to Arrive

Editor: This time my friend went to Suzhou, and I asked him to write to me as soon as he arrived in Suzhou, but there has been no news. I thought my friend had broken his promise, but I did not receive my friend's letter until the 3rd of this month. Looking at the date of dispatch, it was August 25. In the past, friends on the Beijing-Shanghai line would write to me in only three days, and it would only take two days from Shanghai to Pudong. Now it takes three days from Shanghai to Pudong, and it takes nine days for a letter from Suzhou to Pudong. I hope that the postal authorities will improve it as soon as possible. (Chen Ping)

Women and Family Published every Tuesday

Discussion on Knitting

— Huang Peiying

Clothes knitted with wool are very light, warm, and comfortable to wear, making them extremely popular. It's almost impossible to find someone who doesn't have one. Therefore, the knitting business has a broad scope of activity and a bright future. Twenty years ago, I developed a great interest in the knitting business. At that time, in addition to studying various domestic knitting methods, I further researched Japanese knitting methods and gained some experience. In the 17th year of the Republic of China, I established a knitting training center and provided knitting tools, teaching novel knitting methods. At the time, many people came to learn, and the products were very well received. The products were displayed at the National Goods Exhibition of the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and won a special prize certificate and a gold medal. Later, due to the slow pace of handmade products, I referred to the needle-replacing machines used by the Japanese and made inventions and improvements, making the products three times faster than handmade. This type of needle-replacing machine was named the "Wool Knitting Needle Replacer" and was granted a patent by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce of the National Government, obtaining a patent license. It was widely promoted at the time, but since the outbreak of the War of Resistance against Japan, this type of needle-replacing machine could not continue to be manufactured. Although there were plans to manufacture it after the victory, due to various reasons, it has not yet been able to meet readers this year. I cannot help but deeply regret this.

However, handmade knitting only requires carrying a needle and thread, and you can work anytime, anywhere, which has its convenience. However, styles and knitting methods are changing with each passing day. I plan to discuss them with readers in this publication.

How to Knit a Wool Sweater? Two Latest Styles

— Ying

Please look at Ms. Yan Huizhu, the "Queen of Peking Opera." Look at her wearing this latest style wool sweater. Her demeanor is calm, dignified, very beautiful, and elegant.

Tools: Two Peiying No. 9 knitting needles, one sewing needle.

Materials: Two skeins of Double Cat brand dark red yarn, ten skeins of blue yarn.

Stitch count: Six stitches per pattern.

Knitting method: Cast on 160 stitches and knit using a cross-stitch pattern to a height of six inches. Then knit one inch high with dark red, one stitch knit, one stitch purl. At this time, decrease 52 stitches on each side using the decrease method shown in practice figure ten (for the pocket opening). Separately, cast on 48 stitches with two knitting needles and knit in stockinette stitch to a height of six inches. Knit two pieces in the same way (for the pocket flaps). Now connect these two pieces to the decreased sides, continuing with the same blue yarn and original pattern. Afterward, decrease one stitch on each side every half inch, decreasing a total of 22 stitches. Continue to increase one stitch on each side every half inch, increasing a total of 32 stitches. At this time, it is time to shape the armholes. Decrease one stitch on each side every other row, decreasing a total of 40 stitches. Continue to increase one stitch on each side every other row, adding back the 40 stitches that were decreased. (But start increasing stitches when you have knitted two inches high. At this time, you need to shape the neckline. Leave 30 stitches in the center with a needle. Now you need to knit the two sides separately. Leave one stitch at the neckline every row until you have added enough stitches at the armhole. The other side is the same).

Back piece knitting method: Cast on 86 stitches. Knit eight stitches knit one, purl one on one side edge. The rest is still knitted with the same pattern as the front piece, to a height of five inches. Continue to decrease one stitch every half inch on the side that is not knit knit one, purl one, decreasing a total of 15 stitches. Continue to increase one stitch every half inch on the decreased side, increasing a total of 15 stitches. Then shape the armholes in the same way as the front piece, to the same height. The other half of the back piece is knitted in the same way. (But on the edge that is knit eight stitches knit one, purl one, you need to make a buttonhole every three inches (i.e., add one stitch, decrease one stitch). After the front and back pieces are knitted, sew them together using the sewing method in the rear diagram.

Neckline knitting method: Use dark red yarn to knit a one knit, one purl rib for two inches high around the stitches left at the neckline, then bind off. Fold the one inch high rib towards the reverse side and sew it down to make a double layer.

Armhole edge knitting method: Pick up one stitch in each hole around the armhole, picking up a total of 140 stitches. Knit one knit, one purl rib for one inch high (using dark red). The other side is the same.

Belt knitting method: Cast on 13 stitches with dark red yarn and knit one knit, one purl rib to a height of twenty-two inches. Then decrease one stitch on each side every row, decreasing until finished. Make it into a pointed end. Make another one the same way. After knitting, sew them on both sides of the waist on the front piece.

There is also a latest style of wool sweater from 1946. Its style is derived from this year's American clothing samples. It looks even more beautiful and lively when worn by the famous female Peking Opera performer, Tong Zhiling.

Tools: Two Peiying No. 9 knitting needles, one sewing needle.

Materials: Thirteen skeins of Bian Mao brand 4-ply wool yarn.

Knitting method: Cast on 150 stitches, and knit with the same flower pattern as the back, but decrease one stitch on each side every half inch, for a total decrease of forty stitches. Continue to increase one stitch on each side every half inch, for a total increase of thirty-two stitches. At this time, it is necessary to shape the armholes. Decrease one stitch on each side every other row, for a total decrease of thirty-two stitches. Knit for four inches high without increasing or decreasing.

Front panel knitting method: Cast on eighty stitches. Like the back panel, decrease one stitch every half inch for a total of twenty stitches (but when knitting one inch high, knit sixteen stitches on the side that is not decreasing first. From the seventeenth stitch, knit forty-four stitches, knit two, purl two, to a height of one inch, and then bind off these forty-four stitches using the knit-off-stitch method shown in diagram ten. This is the pocket opening.) Use two needles and cast on forty-four stitches for a height of six inches, and then connect it to the middle of the forty-four-stitch pocket opening and knit it together using the original pattern. When one side is decreased to twenty stitches, continue to increase one stitch every half needle, for a total of sixteen stitches. At this time, the armhole should be shaped, the pattern changed, and the neckline shaped. On the side that is flat and not increasing or decreasing, decrease one stitch every three rows from then on, for a total of twenty stitches, to form the neckline (but it must be decreased from the eleventh stitch, because those ten stitches are the center edge; see the rear diagram for the flower pattern knit-off-stitch method). Shape the armhole by decreasing one stitch every other row, for a total decrease of sixteen stitches. Knit until the same height as the back panel. The method for the other side is the same, except that the ten-stitch edge on the front panel must be knit five and a half inches longer, because there is no edge on the back panel neckline. When these ten stitches have been knit to a length of five and a half inches, sew them to the ten stitches on the other side of the front panel. For the remaining stitches, sew the front and back panels together using the sewing method shown in the rear diagram.

Sleeve knitting method: Cast on fifty stitches, and knit with the rice stitch. Afterwards, increase one stitch on each side every other row, for a total of fifty stitches. Continue knitting for eleven inches without increasing or decreasing. Then, in one row, decrease forty stitches (i.e., decrease one stitch, decrease one stitch, knit one stitch, and so on.) so that one hundred stitches remain sixty stitches. Continue knitting for three and a half inches, knit two, purl one. The knitting method for the other sleeve is the same. When sewing it onto the garment, if the top of the sleeve is too large, it can be slightly puffed up on the shoulder blade.

Belt knitting method: Cast on nine stitches and knit with the rice stitch to a height of twenty-eight inches. Continue to decrease one stitch on each side every other row, decreasing until finished. Make it into a pointed end.

After the garment is completely knitted, embroider it on the left side of the front panel according to the embroidery pattern. Whatever design you like, you can embroider it as you like. The color scheme can also be as you like.

Washing and Preserving Wool Products

— Pei

The Special Qualities of Wool: Before discussing how to wash wool products, we should first know the special qualities of wool. The main component of wool, the wool fiber, has what is called an outer scale, which must not be rubbed vigorously. If rubbed too vigorously, the fluff on the wool yarn will form clumps, losing its original beauty. Wool yarns have a very weak alkaline reaction, so you must use high-quality soap when washing them, otherwise the wool yarn will easily become stiff. If you are washing colored wool yarn, and there is a possibility of fading when washing, you must first use a color-fixing method before washing. The color-fixing method is to mix one teaspoon of tannic acid and one teaspoon of acetic acid in one liter of clean water, put the item to be washed in it and soak for five or six minutes, and then wash it.

Washing Method: The washing method is to first remove the dust, so wash it in clear water. After washing three or four times, put it in soapy water and move it up, down, left, and right. Afterwards, rinse it with clean water and then use the acid-through method. The acid-through method has the effect of protecting the luster of the wool and preventing damage to the wool, so you must perform the acid-through method at the end of washing wool products. The acid-through method is very simple. You can put half a glass of acetic acid or two glasses of ordinary vinegar in one liter of clean water to make acidic water. Put the washed item in it and soak for five or six minutes, and then take it out and dry it.

Drying Method: The drying method cannot be like other things where you squeeze it dry vigorously. After the acid-through method, take it out and place it on a flat board to stretch it out, then smooth the shape, and then tilt the board up and place it in a cool, shady place to dry, so you can maintain the original beauty of the item.

Preservation Method: As for the preservation method, the most important thing is to prevent insect infestation and to prevent the item from discoloring and deteriorating. The first method of insect prevention is to wash all the stains completely before storing it, which will be effective. At the same time, the washed item must be fully dried and must be stored in a dry place. When storing, each item should be wrapped separately in paper, and camphor or mothballs should be placed in the middle, and they must be wrapped in thin paper bags to prevent the powder from camphor, etc., from getting stuck in the seams and being difficult to remove. After wrapping them like this, store them in a cabinet or box, and then place the box in a dry, shady place, and do not let the sun shine directly on it, so you can prevent discoloration and deterioration.

Mother First

— Yinguo

The "women's liberation" movement of the past ten years has indeed seen some women doing things that benefit the community, no less than men. But unfortunately, most women, especially urban women, after being "liberated," not only continue to live a dependent life, but even no longer want to be as submissive as before, but only know how to enjoy rights and do not want to fulfill obligations, and have even broken down the concept of "virtuous wife and good mother."

Children are the cornerstone of future society and the pillars of the country. If we want the future country and society to become more perfect, we must do our best to promote children's education.

The education that children receive in school is mechanical and limited, and teachers cannot follow students all day long to teach them at any time. Therefore, the education of children should be the equal responsibility of parents and teachers. In school, it is the teacher's responsibility, and at home, it should be the parents' responsibility. Especially mothers, because children have more frequent contact with their mothers than with their fathers, there is no doubt that children's will and temperament will tend to follow their mother's teachings and instructions. In the corners of the city, it is easy to see that when a mother is engrossed in gambling or playing outside all day long, they easily give their children money and hand over the responsibility of supervision to servants, or let their children associate with the lower classes. Of course, "those who are near vermilion get stained red, and those who are near ink get stained black," and the children will learn everything: gambling, swearing…

Raising a child is like cultivating a flower or grass. If it is cared for, cherished, and planted by a diligent gardener, it will always thrive. On the contrary, if it encounters a lazy gardener who lets it be exposed to the sun and rain without pruning its branches, there is no doubt that this flower or grass will eventually wither.

Look at the great men of the world. Their success is almost always influenced by their mother's diligent teaching, because they can use their observational skills to identify the child's psychology, grasp the child's emotions, and instill pure ideas to cultivate and correct them.

Of course, not every mother in the world can raise their children into great men, but at least they should not raise parasites that are of no use to society, the community, or the country.

May all mothers in the world take on this great responsibility!

Reasoning with Children

— Yimin

(1) It's Not Just the Rose That's Like This

In my grandmother's garden, there was a rose that had already grown buds, but it didn't bloom for many days. This made me feel very impatient, because I was eager to see its beautiful petals and colors. I prepared to give it a helping hand and make it bloom. With my grandmother's permission, I unfolded its petals one by one. In the end, the rose seemed to bloom, but it was not as beautiful and moving as I had seen before. Undoubtedly, the rose's inherent beauty was destroyed by me, and it quickly withered and died. My grandmother saw it and said to me gently, "Everything is like this. Roses can only produce beautiful flowers in a certain order and at a certain time."

(2) The Lesson of the Basket

The six children in our family always liked to talk about other people's private affairs, spreading gossip, which was harmful to others and not beneficial to themselves. Our father hated our bad habit very much. One day, he brought back a package and said, "I bought each of you a small basket. When you have something to talk about, write it down and put it in your basket. After the basket is full, you can examine it one by one and see how much meaning there is. At first, we thought it was a ridiculous job, but soon we became very careful about what we said. After a while, we simply forgot about this bad habit of talking about others. Later, our father explained, "This little basket has become your monitor. Now you will no longer bring nonsense from school, the office, or the factory to harm others. Although your baskets are empty, they are more meaningful than when they were full."

Good Wife

— Translated by Gangren

No matter what you think, you are not the good wife you should be if: —

You tell your friends: "It's so annoying! My husband he…."

You dress up more carefully when you go out alone to attend a party than when your husband accompanies you to see a movie.

You prefer to tell your husband how hard you have worked all day, rather than tell him how these work experiences have added to your enjoyment.

When you want to chat with your own friends, you leave your husband and family unattended.

You tell your husband the bad news at dinner, not when you know your husband is in a good mood.

You are never satisfied with the house you currently live in and always want new things to make it more beautiful.

You decorate your "home" well, and seem to value your friends' praise more than the comfort your husband gets from it.

You have no interest in entertaining your husband's friends.

You would rather choose your own gifts yourself than take the "risk" that he might buy you something you don't like.

You often say: "I want my husband to do this and that," instead of saying: "I hope he can do this and that, if he is willing."

You never let your husband get the credit for a certain opinion until he has done it well.

You never ask your husband's opinion about anything. (Originally published in The China Press)

How to Manage Servants

— Yuan

Every housewife who manages a household must supervise her servants at all times and see if their measures and actions are appropriate. She must not neglect them. The method of supervision should have common sense. Then, when she speaks and gives orders, she will be able to be fair and just, so that the servants will obey and behave without any actions that go beyond the norm. The following are several points that a housewife should have knowledge of. Readers should consider them carefully and supplement them with experience. You will naturally be able to achieve the subtlety of commanding at will!

When selecting servants, only seek diligence and simplicity, and be sure to examine their nature to see if they can obey the master's orders? Do not judge based on the amount of wages. Honest servants are diligent in their work and benefit the master in no small way. It is appropriate for them to demand a good price. As for lazy and dissolute people, who steal time and enjoy leisure, or are stubborn and difficult to train, even if the wages are low, the gains and losses are not enough to offset them. Therefore, the best servants are those who are diligent and thrifty, and who are gentle in nature and have no heart of arrogance or rudeness. This is considered qualified. Conversely, it is not easy to manage them. Even if they have special skills, they should not be hired, lest they cause trouble later.

For people living at home, clean clothes and utensils are the most important thing, and so are servants. Gorgeous clothes are not appropriate, and damaged and dirty clothes are also unsightly. The reason why clothes are dirty and tattered is not because of poverty, but mostly because of laziness and laziness in washing and mending. As the saying goes, "The effort of one stitch, when sewing is timely, is enough to save the labor of nine stitches." If a servant does not know how to clean themselves, it is impossible to expect them to be diligent in other things. It is like climbing a tree to catch fish, which is impossible. As for servants flaunting their clothes and dressing up like their mistresses, it is also not appropriate. The master should patiently guide them, teach them to save, and explain the benefits and harms of extravagance. She should tell them that the money earned from labor is very little and should not be wasted at will. She should also tell them that people who earn a living through physical labor sometimes have to stop working, or they may suddenly suffer from old age or illness, and they will need money for support. If they do not save regularly, when something happens, they will not know where to get it in a hurry. In general, all hired workers should be diligent and thrifty and not be extravagant. If clothes are torn, they should be mended, not thrown away. They should not indulge in eating and drinking. As for shopping and socializing, they should also be restrained at all times to save money. As the ancient saying goes, "Saving one penny is the same as earning one penny." Otherwise, if they indulge in their desires without satisfaction, they will inevitably fall into extravagance, and when the money is gone and they are empty-handed, they will have improper thoughts. When they reach the end of the road, it will be too late to regret their mistakes!

The duties that servants should perform are numerous and cannot be listed one by one, such as cooking, washing, sweeping, and cleaning utensils, and caring for children. All of these are their duties. However, cooking and washing each have specific duties, which cannot be explained in a simple way. In wealthy families, there are many servants, and each has their own job, such as cooks and wet nurses. Even if this is not the case, the master must assign their duties and cannot entrust everything to one person. However, sweeping and cleaning the house and cleaning the utensils are the usual duties of servants. Now let me talk about them as follows:

Get up at dawn, open the windows and doors, and roll up the curtains to let fresh air into the room. If it is winter, and there is a stove in the room, you must first remove the ashes and leftover charcoal, and then sweep the floor. When removing the ashes, the technique should be gentle, and it is best to cover the gold and porcelain utensils, chairs, and wall clothes in the room with cloth to prevent dust from collecting. When sweeping the floor, first sprinkle water on it, which can also reduce the spread of dust. After sweeping, wipe the windows. All glass cabinets, fences, and the edges of mirrors and picture frames must be wiped. If there are copper or steel utensils, they should be rubbed with soft leather to prevent them from rusting. If rust is seen, it must be sanded with sandpaper or coated with lime, and it must be smooth before stopping. Other items, such as tables, chairs, and frames, must be wiped so that there are no stains left. All of these things should be done before the master gets up. Once the master gets up, the bedroom must be cleaned, the bedding must be spread, and it must be swept and wiped as described above.

If there are vases or water-filled basins in the room, they must be emptied and refilled with clean water every day.

Every few days, the quilts and pillows should be exposed to the sun. Other things, such as sweeping the stairs or beating the carpets, must be done on sunny days and when you have free time. Do not annoy the master. In the evening, close the windows and lock the doors. Do not be lazy or forgetful. These are also the duties of servants.

The above is only a brief discussion, but you must provide guidance in a proper way so that you can enjoy the benefits. If there are any mistakes, you must gently persuade them and show them kindness so that the servants will return with gratitude and be sincerely convinced. Otherwise, even if you spend a lot of money, you will not be able to buy their loyalty, which is not the best policy.

Save the Unfortunate Children Made by Man

— Chen Xin

There are many unfortunate children in China. They are children who have encountered natural disasters or man-made disasters, lost their parents at an early age, or been abandoned and are wandering around. These unfortunate children should receive widespread sympathy from people.

However, people have not noticed that in addition to these unfortunate children, there are more unfortunate children made by man. That is, when the children's father or mother has an affair, the children's unfortunate fate begins. In the current semi-feudal society, there are not many women who are mothers who have affairs, but it is common for men to do so.

My previous ideal was that a healthy marriage could definitely build a happy family, and that a new generation would be happy and excellent. But reality shattered my ideal. I have personally seen that between friends and relatives, they used to have a long and sweet love process, and their personalities cannot be said to be misunderstood. Moreover, they are both intellectuals who serve society. But after marriage, even after ten or twenty years, when they have "green shades and full branches of children," the hardworking mother is old and her beauty has faded; but the father's career is gradually leading to success. Generally, men who are fickle-minded, with status and money, will find a concubine or mistress. They only see the new person smiling, but they don't hear the old person crying. They don't care about destroying the family's happiness, and they don't experience or think about the psychological impact on the children, because they are becoming more and more distant from the children.

Chinese women, who have always been influenced by traditional rituals and teachings, even those who have been baptized by new ideas, will never casually shout for divorce. When she suffers this unexpected blow, the gentle ones will silently entrust their hopes and love to the next generation. But this broken heart that has been stimulated will sometimes become abnormally unreasonable and vent on the children, beating, scolding, and even ignoring them. The children, facing this family shrouded in haze, have inexplicable hatred and jealousy in their innocent and weak hearts. They cannot get the warmth of home, and they lose their great father's love. Their small hearts are being destroyed.

If the mother has a fierce and irritable personality, she will definitely quarrel with her husband, and because she uses retaliatory measures, she will roam outside all day long, using cinemas and dance halls to numb her heart that has lost joy. As a result, these "fatherless and motherless" children are not well-fed and clothed, and they often suffer from hunger and cold in winter. They have no home except to make trouble in the lanes all day long. When they occasionally see their parents, it is either a cold face or a fight. Under such family education, the spiritual and material education that the children receive is perhaps even worse than that of orphans without parents.

If we want to raise an excellent second generation, we must hold the fathers responsible for most of their responsibilities. Fathers should restrain their selfish lust and irrigate the new seedlings with great fatherly love. I also hope that every woman can respect her own personality, strengthen her reason, and not be seduced by men. It is dishonorable and base to be a concubine. It is not protected by law, and it is disdained by women of the new era. What's more, destroying other people's families and harming the second generation of the new China, you are committing crimes that harm society and the community!

We must save these unfortunate children!

Goethe's Later Years

— Mai Fo

Thomas Mann and "Lover's Return"

In the history of world literature, there is no giant more brilliant than Goethe. For Chinese readers, who can forget his masterpiece "The Sorrows of Young Werther"? This is an autobiographical novel of his. After its publication, it was as sought after as the paper of Luoyang, and it spread like wildfire. Many young people heartbroken in love committed suicide with a copy of "The Sorrows of Young Werther" in their hands.

In the spring of 1772, at the young age of twenty-two, the young Goethe set off for Wetzlar, a town in central Germany, to do a legal internship at the Imperial Court. At the age of sixteen, he left his hometown of Frankfurt and studied law in Leipzig and Strasbourg. During this period, he fell ill and stayed at home for a while. In Leipzig, he fell in love with Käthchen Schönkopf, and in Strasbourg, he fell passionately for Friederike Brion, both ending in separation. These formed the model for Goethe's early love affairs, separations, and regrets. Now, Goethe arrived in Wetzlar with a large number of poems, plays, sketches, and

Ideal Wife and Ideal Husband

— Li Xin

[Editor's Note: In our August 30th issue, Mr. Zhiwei's "My Ideal Wife" was published, outlining the conditions for his future wife. Many readers responded to this issue, and some even requested that their letters be forwarded to Mr. Zhiwei, which shows the urgent interest young friends have in marriage. Here, we have selected a few letters from those received and published them below, which may be helpful for young people hesitating at the crossroads of love.]

When people reach a certain age, choosing a lifelong partner is an important matter; however, everyone has different ideals.

I believe that the ideal husband should possess the following qualities:

A proper appearance and neat attire, but not excessively decorated; not worshiping fashion and rushing to buy glass trouser belts and other such items. This is beauty in appearance.

Not having bad habits such as "smoking," "drinking," "prostitution," and "gambling"; demanding the improvement of "intellect," "physical fitness," "morality," and "[character]" cultivation. This is beauty in nature.

A strong body, a lively spirit, and no potentially hereditary or contagious diseases. This is physiological beauty.

Excellent knowledge, having received at least twelve years of education; being courageous in service, having a spirit of self-sacrifice, and possessing clear judgment and independent thinking. This is beauty in knowledge and behavior.

Only an "ideal husband" can marry an "ideal wife," do you think that's right?

Not Buying Something

— Xiao Wei

I sigh at the excessive "self-centeredness" of human nature in this world, which causes all kinds of conflicts and battles, each with its own set of rigid rules, wanting the world to follow and conform to it. Extreme ideologues do not hesitate to use bloodshed to make the world conform to them all at once, but as a result, humanity suffers before it can enjoy the benefits. I am deeply concerned about the issue of marriage, but I am opposed to both sides listing out conditions. Choosing a partner should not be done carelessly, but it is not entirely like buying something.

A Letter of Self-Recommendation

— Xu Yeye

Mr. Zhiwei:

I don't know why, but I finally decided to write this letter. In this mountain city where feudal colors are still strong, this move seems almost absurd, but because of this, please do not underestimate it.

Self-introduction:

I am a graduate of a vocational school. I love my work, and I never forget to learn, so that I can better understand the needs of my time.

I dare only say that within my small circle of life, I can handle things calmly.

Regarding the three words "Truth, Goodness, Beauty," would you like to explain them in detail? How can life step into the realm of "Truth, Goodness, Beauty"? However, regardless of these, I want to make life simple, gentle, and without intense charm?

My face is very ordinary! Sir, the women here are very simple, even simpler than your five, six, or seven ideals, and naturally I am no exception.

I can probably manage a small family well.

Traveling is my only hobby.

Based on the above points, regardless of whether there are any major differences with you, I always hope to be friends with you from a different place and of the opposite sex. I have never been to a bustling city, especially Shanghai, which is known as heaven on earth. I would very much like to meet you there. Although I have no contribution to make to you, I can always report on things that are not found in bustling places.
